### [36] [HiGS: A Hierarchical Rendering Architecture for Real-Time 3D Gaussian Splatting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00352)
*Dawid Pająk,Martin Bisson,Rodolfo Lima*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: HiGS introduces hierarchical tiling to decouple spatial partitioning and rasterization in 3D Gaussian Splatting, enabling faster rendering by using coarse macro-tiles for partitioning and fine tiles for rasterization. This allows work distribution proportional to gaussian density, reducing bottlenecks in dense regions. HiGS achieves up to 15.8x speedup over original 3DGS and outperforms other rasterizers while maintaining exact alpha compositing.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The original 3DGS pipeline couples spatial partitioning and rasterization to a single tile size, creating a trade-off: larger tiles reduce partitioning cost but increase rasterization cost, and vice versa. Dense tiles become bottlenecks as they serialize processing, limiting performance.

Method: HiGS uses hierarchically tiled rendering: coarse macro-tiles handle spatial partitioning and depth sorting, while fine render tiles perform rasterization within each macro-tile. Rasterization tasks are assigned proportionally to the number of gaussians per macro-tile, enabling better load balancing across parallel units.

Result: HiGS achieves up to 15.8x faster rendering than original 3DGS across tested scenes, outperforms all evaluated rasterizers, and maintains exact front-to-back alpha compositing without approximation.

Conclusion: By decoupling partitioning and rasterization through hierarchical tiling, HiGS effectively resolves the scalability bottleneck in 3DGS, enabling high-performance real-time novel view synthesis on commodity GPUs while preserving visual fidelity.

Abstract: 3D Gaussian Splatting (3DGS) has become the standard for real-time novel view synthesis on commodity GPUs. Its pipeline ties spatial partitioning and rasterization to one tile size, yet the two pull in opposite directions: partitioning, which bins and depth-sorts gaussians, grows cheaper with larger tiles, while rasterization gets cheaper with smaller ones. Prior acceleration work reduces the cost of individual stages but keeps both locked to that single scale, where a few dense tiles dominate frame time. We present Hierarchically Tiled Gaussian Splatting (HiGS), which gives each its own scale: partitioning runs over coarse macro-tiles, while rasterization runs over the fine render tiles within them. Rasterization work is then issued in proportion to the gaussians in each macro-tile rather than per tile, so dense regions spread across many parallel units instead of serializing through one. Across tested scenes, HiGS renders up to 15.8x faster than the original 3DGS and outperforms every other rasterizer we evaluate, while preserving exact front-to-back alpha compositing.

</details>


### [37] [LFA: Layer Feature Attention for Run-Time Introspection of 2D Object Detectors in Automated Driving](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00372)
*Mert Keser,Alois Knoll*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为层特征注意力（LFA）的轻量级内省方法，通过注意力机制聚合骨干网络多层特征，以提升目标检测错误预测的准确性。该方法利用不同层次特征在视觉抽象上的差异：低层捕捉细粒度信息，高层提供语义理解，从而更全面地识别检测失败。实验表明，LFA在KITTI和BDD100K数据集上均优于现有单层方法，具有更强的性能和可解释性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有内省方法仅依赖最后一层特征或手工设计统计量，忽略了早期层中蕴含的重要视觉信息，导致对检测错误的预测能力受限。

Method: 提出层特征注意力（LFA）方法，通过端到端学习多层骨干网络特征的重要性权重，利用注意力机制融合不同层次的特征表示，实现更精准的错误预测与可解释性分析。

Result: 在KITTI和BDD100K数据集上的实验结果显示，LFA在多种检测器架构下均达到当前最优的内省性能，显著优于基于单一层次特征的方法。

Conclusion: LFA通过有效利用多层特征信息，实现了更准确、可解释的检测器内省，为自动驾驶中的安全部署提供了可靠支持。

Abstract: Reliable object detection is critical for automated driving, yet even state-of-the-art detectors inevitably make errors that can compromise safety. Introspection methods that predict detector failures enable safer deployment by triggering fallback mechanisms or alerting human operators. However, existing approaches rely solely on last-layer features or hand-crafted statistics, discarding valuable information from earlier layers that capture different levels of visual abstraction. We propose Layer Feature Attention (LFA), a lightweight introspection method that learns to aggregate features from multiple backbone layers through an attention mechanism. Our key insight is that detection errors manifest differently across feature hierarchies: low-level layers capture fine-grained details essential for detecting small or occluded objects, while high-level layers encode semantic information for scene understanding. LFA learns layer importance weights end-to-end, enabling both improved error prediction and interpretable analysis of which feature levels are most indicative of detector failures. Extensive experiments on KITTI and BDD100K demonstrate that LFA achieves state-of-the-art introspection performance, outperforming single-layer baselines across multiple detector architectures.

</details>


### [38] [Score-Control for Hallucination Reduction in Diffusion Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00377)
*Mahesh Bhosale,Naresh Kumar Devulapally,Abdul Wasi,Chau Pham,Vishnu Suresh Lokhande,David Doermann*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了扩散模型中幻觉现象与得分函数平滑性之间的关系，提出一种基于方差引导的得分调制（VSM）策略，通过控制得分雅可比矩阵来降低得分平滑性，从而减少幻觉并提升生成图像的可靠性。实验表明，该方法在真实和合成数据集上可将幻觉减少约25%，同时保持高质量和多样性。此外，研究还构建了两个具有极端语义变化的基准数据集以系统评估幻觉问题。代码与数据集已公开。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扩散模型虽在多模态生成任务中表现卓越，但其生成结果常出现超出真实数据分布范围的幻觉样本，影响模型可靠性与可信度。现有研究推测得分平滑性是导致幻觉的原因之一，但缺乏系统验证与理论支撑。因此，亟需从理论和方法层面深入理解并解决该问题。

Method: 首先通过实证验证得分平滑性导致幻觉的假设，并引入密度视角进行解释；进一步建立幻觉概率质量与学习得分函数的Lipschitz常数之间的理论关联；据此提出变方差引导得分调制（VSM）策略，通过调节得分函数的雅可比结构，抑制过度平滑，逼近真实得分函数，从而减少幻觉。

Result: 在合成与真实世界数据集上的实验表明，所提方法能有效降低幻觉发生率（最高达~25%），同时保持高保真度与多样性。所提出的两个新基准数据集为幻觉评估提供了系统化工具。

Conclusion: 本研究从理论与实践双重视角揭示了得分平滑性与幻觉之间的内在联系，提出的VSM策略为构建更可靠、可信的扩散生成模型提供了有效路径，推动了生成式AI的稳健性发展。

Abstract: Diffusion models have emerged as the backbone of modern generative AI, powering advances in vision, language, audio and other modalities. Despite their success, they suffer from hallucinations, implausible samples that lie outside the support of true data distribution, which degrade reliability and trust. In this work, we first empirically confirm previously proposed hypothesis that score smoothness causes hallucinations in Image Generation diffusion models and provide a density-based perspective. We further formalize this notion by linking the hallucinations probability mass to lipschitz constant of the learned score function. Motivated by this, we introduce a Variance-Guided Score Modulation (VSM) strategy that controls the score Jacobian, in turn reducing score smoothness and better approximating the ground truth score that decreases hallucinations. Empirical results on synthetic and real-world datasets demonstrate that our approach reduces hallucinations (up to ~25%) while maintaining high fidelity and diversity, providing a principled step toward more reliable diffusion-based image generation. We also propose two benchmark datasets with extreme semantic variation for systematic hallucination evaluation. Code and Datasets are publicly available at https://github.com/bhosalems/VSM.

</details>


### [39] [Non-Learning Low-Light Stereo Vision](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00379)
*Jason Wang,Lucas Nguyen,Hyunseung Eom,Wei Xu,Qi Guo*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出了一种非学习的立体框架，用于从严重噪声图像中进行视差估计。该方法利用结点场（FoJ）保留受严重噪声影响较小的粗略视觉特征，用于构建代价体，同时丢弃与光子噪声难以区分的细纹理。由此产生的结构信息指导边界感知的半全局匹配（SGM），动态调整平滑性惩罚以保护真实的视差不连续性。最终输出的稀疏视差图在未遮挡像素上比近期立体算法更准确，且在广泛使用的基准数据集上表现优异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有立体匹配方法在严重噪声图像上性能下降，因细纹理易被噪声干扰，导致代价体构建不准确。需要一种能够保留稳定结构信息、抑制噪声影响的方法，以提高视差估计精度。

Method: 采用结点场（FoJ）提取图像中的粗略结构特征，忽略受噪声影响大的细纹理；基于这些结构信息构建代价体，并结合边界感知的半全局匹配（SGM），动态调整平滑性惩罚以保持真实视差边界。

Result: 在多个标准基准数据集上，该方法在未遮挡区域的视差估计精度优于当前主流立体算法，生成的稀疏视差图具有更高的准确性。

Conclusion: 所提出的非学习框架有效应对了严重噪声下的立体匹配挑战，通过保留稳定结构信息并动态调节平滑约束，显著提升了视差估计的鲁棒性和精度。

Abstract: We present a non-learning stereo framework for disparity estimation from severely noisy images. Using the Field of Junctions (FoJ), it retains coarse visual features stable under severe noise for cost volume construction while discarding fine textures inseparable from photon noise. The resulting structural information guides boundary-aware Semi-Global Matching (SGM) that dynamically adapts smoothness penalties to preserve true disparity discontinuities. The output is a sparse disparity map more accurate than those of recent stereo algorithms over unmasked pixels on widely-used benchmark datasets.

### [40] [SUPREME: A Multi-GPU Framework for Reproducible Image Unlearning Method Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00380)
*Petros Andreou,Jamie Lanyon,Axel Finke,Georgina Cosma*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: SUPREME是一个开源框架，通过多GPU分布式计算加速机器遗忘的评估过程，支持多种模型、方法和场景，显著提升效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有图像分类遗忘框架受限于单个GPU，导致评估多个随机种子时计算成本过高，无法在合理时间内完成大量实验。

Method: 采用基于注册表的设计，支持灵活扩展新方法、指标、模型和场景；设计多GPU架构，可并行处理训练、遗忘和评估任务，并支持多种加速器和精度模式。

Result: 在10个随机种子上对Pins人脸识别任务进行全类和随机样本遗忘实验，使用ResNet18和ViT模型验证了框架的有效性与高效性。

Abstract: Machine unlearning removes the influence of specific training data from a trained model without retraining it from scratch. Evaluating an unlearning method requires repeating training, unlearning, and evaluation across multiple seeds, which is computationally expensive. To our knowledge, existing image classification unlearning frameworks run on a single GPU, which limits how many seeds can be evaluated in reasonable time. We introduce SUPREME, an open-source framework that distributes these stages across multiple GPUs. SUPREME makes three contributions: a registry-based design for adding new methods, metrics, models, and scenarios; a multi-GPU architecture supporting multiple accelerators and precision modes; and a demonstration on Pins Face Recognition using ResNet18 and ViT under full-class and random-sample unlearning across ten seeds. The framework is available at https://github.com/pedroandreou/supreme-unlearning.

### [41] [αDepth: Learning Single-Pass Soft Boundary Decomposition for Stereo Conversion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00386)
*Xiang Zhang,Yang Zhang,Lukas Mehl,Karlis Martins Briedis,Markus Gross,Christopher Schroers*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出αDepth，一种用于立体转换的分层表示方法，通过在软边界处估计分层的颜色和深度值来解决颜色与深度的混合模糊问题。引入圆形透明度表示（CAR），将全局目标提取转变为局部边界分解，实现无需人工干预的场景级推理，显著提升复杂多目标场景下的立体转换质量，有效消除背景渗漏和结构失真。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有深度模型在软边界（如头发、散焦模糊）处因单一深度预测导致深度对应模糊；传统抠图方法在复杂多目标场景中表现不佳且需人工干预，难以满足高保真立体转换需求。

Method: 提出αDepth分层表示，结合分层颜色与深度估计以解决混合模糊；设计圆形透明度表示（CAR），实现从全局目标提取到局部边界分解的范式转变，支持无监督的场景级推理。

Result: 在多个基准测试中达到当前最佳性能，显著改善软边界处的立体转换效果，有效消除背景渗漏与结构失真，适用于复杂多目标场景。

Conclusion: αDepth通过分层建模与创新的CAR表示，实现了高保真立体转换，尤其在软边界处理上优于现有方法，为复杂场景下的立体视觉重建提供了新思路。

Abstract: Accurately modeling soft boundaries, e.g., hair and defocus blur, is a fundamental challenge in stereo conversion due to the ambiguous blending of foreground and background. Existing depth models primarily predict single-layer depth, leading to ambiguity in depth correspondence at soft boundaries. While matting techniques can capture opacity for layered modeling, they often struggle in complex scenes with multiple targets and usually require user intervention. This paper introduces αDepth, a layered representation that decomposes soft boundaries for high-fidelity stereo conversion. Specifically, we first resolve mixed color and depth ambiguity by estimating layered color and depth values at soft boundaries. Considering complex multi-target scenes, we design a Circular Alpha Representation (CAR) that shifts the paradigm from global target extraction to local boundary decomposition. Unlike prior matting methods restricted to a single foreground/background, CAR enables efficient scene-level inference without manual guidance. Extensive evaluations demonstrate that αDepth achieves state-of-the-art performance in stereo conversion, eliminating background bleeding and structural distortions at soft boundaries.

### [42] [Zamba2-VL Technical Report](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00390)
*Hassan Shapourian,Kasra Hejazi,Olabode M. Sule,Beren Millidge*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: Zamba2-VL 是基于 Zamba2 架构的视觉-语言模型，结合了 Mamba2 状态空间层与少量共享 Transformer 块，具备高效推理能力。在图像理解、推理、OCR、定位和计数等任务上表现媲美主流 Transformer-based 开源模型（如 Molmo2、Qwen3-VL、InternVL3.5），且显著优于先前基于 SSM 或混合架构的 VLM。其核心优势在于近线性预填充计算和小而恒定的循环状态，使在相同参数量下，首令牌生成时间（TTFT）比 Transformer 模型低约一个数量级，尤其在 1.2B 和 2.7B 小规模模型上对边缘部署更具优势。作者发布了三个版本（1.2B、2.7B、7B）及推理代码。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 提升视觉-语言模型的推理效率，尤其是在资源受限的设备上实现快速响应，同时保持高性能。现有 Transformer-based 模型虽性能优异但计算开销大，而早期 SSM-based 模型在性能上仍有不足。因此需要一种兼具高效率与强性能的新型架构。

Method: 采用 Zamba2 的混合架构，融合 Mamba2 状态空间层与少量共享 Transformer 块，构建视觉-语言模型。利用 Mamba2 的近线性计算特性与小而稳定的递归状态，优化推理延迟，同时通过结构设计保留足够的表达能力以支持复杂视觉-语言任务。

Result: Zamba2-VL 在多个基准测试中达到与主流 Transformer-based 模型相当的性能，且在推理速度上显著领先，特别是在小规模模型上，首令牌生成时间（TTFT）降低约一个数量级，适合边缘和设备端部署。

Conclusion: Zamba2-VL 成功实现了高效与高性能的平衡，证明了混合架构在视觉-语言建模中的潜力，尤其适用于对延迟敏感的应用场景，为轻量化、高效率的多模态模型发展提供了新路径。

Abstract: We present Zamba2-VL, a suite of vision-language models built on Zamba2, a hybrid language-model architecture combining Mamba2 state-space layers with a small number of shared transformer blocks. Across a broad range of image understanding, reasoning, OCR, grounding, and counting benchmarks, Zamba2-VL is competitive with leading Transformer-based open-weight VLMs of comparable scale, including the Molmo2, Qwen3-VL, and InternVL3.5 families, and substantially outperforms prior SSM-based and hybrid VLMs such as VL-Mamba, Cobra, and mmMamba. Inheriting the near-linear prefill compute and small, near-constant recurrent state of its Zamba2 backbone, Zamba2-VL delivers roughly an order of magnitude lower time-to-first-token (TTFT) than these Transformer baselines at matched parameter scale, with the efficiency gap most pronounced at the smaller 1.2B and 2.7B scales most relevant to on-device and edge deployment. We release three models -- 1.2B, 2.7B, and 7B -- together with inference code at https://huggingface.co/collections/Zyphra/zamba2-vl.

### [43] [Rethinking Amortized Neural Representations for High-Resolution Terrain Elevation Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00404)
*Haoan Feng,Xin Xu,Leila De Floriani*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出一种针对地形高程数据的高效神经表示方法HUVR+SIREN，通过改进超网络结构并使用可解析微分的坐标解码器，在不增加每块存储开销的情况下实现更优的高度和导数保真度，并支持高压缩量化，适用于大规模地形数据的紧凑神经格式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有隐式神经表示（INRs）在处理大规模地形数据时因需为每块独立训练和存储模型而难以扩展；虽然有压缩方法如超网络能降低存储成本，但其在地形数据上的表现尚未明确，且多数方法源自自然图像领域，不适合地形的连续平滑特性。

Method: 构建了一个1米/像素的地形数据基准测试集，评估三种代表性方法；在此基础上提出HUVR+SIREN，将最强方法HUVR中的坐标解码器替换为平滑、可解析微分的SIREN结构，提升对地形表面建模的能力。

Result: HUVR+SIREN在高度与导数保真度上优于其他方法，无需额外每块存储，解码成本更低，且在极端量化下仍保持高质量，验证了其作为紧凑地形神经格式的有效性。

Conclusion: 当前每块瓶颈已接近极限，剩余性能差距源于共享超网络架构设计不足，表明未来优化应聚焦于超网络本身的结构改进而非每块编码器。

Abstract: Implicit neural representations (INRs) model a signal as a continuous coordinate-to-value function. For terrain elevation data, this supports analytic derivatives, arbitrary-resolution decoding, and a smooth surface model of the underlying heightfield. However, fitting and storing a separate INR for every tile does not scale to large terrain datasets. Amortized neural representations reduce this cost with a shared network: a new tile is mapped to a compact per-tile payload, and a shared decoder reconstructs the heightfield from it. Most such methods are hypernetworks that predict the payload in a single forward pass, while others recover it through a short per-tile optimization. These methods were developed primarily for natural images, and their suitability for terrain heightfields remains unclear. We introduce a controlled benchmark on a 1 m/pixel terrain dataset and evaluate three representative methods under a unified protocol. Observing a clear cross-domain gap, we propose HUVR+SIREN, a hypernetwork that adapts the strongest benchmarked method (HUVR) by replacing its coordinate decoder with a smooth, analytically differentiable one. It attains the best height and derivative fidelity on the benchmark with no additional per-tile storage and lower decode cost, and tolerates aggressive post-training quantization with negligible quality loss, giving a compact terrain neural format. Ablations and diagnostics further identify which design choices transfer to terrain and show that the per-tile bottleneck is already near its useful limit, leaving the remaining gap in the shared hypernetwork's architectural design.

</details>


### [44] [4D Radar Meets LiDAR and Camera: Cooperative Perception under Adverse Weather](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00416)
*Melih Yazgan,Iramm Hamdard,Qiyuan Wu,J. Marius Zoellner*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 该研究提出一种基于4D成像雷达的协作感知方法，通过引入多普勒引导的空间注意力机制，在恶劣天气下提升摄像头与激光雷达性能退化的鲁棒性。研究扩展了两种典型骨干网络：雷达-相机管道（雷达替代激光雷达）和激光雷达-雷达管道（雷达补充激光雷达），并发布了两个增强雷达数据集（OPV2V-R 和 Adver-City-R），用于评估在物理模拟激光雷达退化条件下的表现。实验表明，该方法在雾和雨天中表现出显著的鲁棒性提升，尤其当雷达替代失效的激光雷达时效果更优；在MAN TruckScenes数据集上的验证进一步证明其可迁移性。整体结果表明，4D成像雷达是全天候协作感知的关键可靠模态。

Motivation: 现有协作感知系统在恶劣天气下因摄像头和激光雷达性能下降而变得脆弱，亟需一种对天气变化不敏感的传感器融合方案以保障自动驾驶系统的稳定性与安全性。

Method: 提出一种基于4D成像雷达的协作感知框架，引入多普勒引导的空间注意力机制实现多智能体信息融合；设计两种融合架构：雷达-相机管道（雷达替代激光雷达）和激光雷达-雷达管道（雷达互补激光雷达）；构建具有物理基础的激光雷达退化模拟数据集进行评估。

Result: 在雾和雨等恶劣天气条件下，系统表现出显著的感知鲁棒性提升；当激光雷达失效时，由雷达替代可大幅改善感知性能；在真实世界数据集MAN TruckScenes上也验证了方法的泛化能力。

Conclusion: 4D成像雷达是一种极具潜力的天气鲁棒型传感器，能够有效支撑全天候环境下的协作感知系统，为自动驾驶在复杂气象条件下的安全运行提供关键技术保障。

Abstract: Cooperative perception is important for autonomous driving but remains fragile when cameras and LiDAR degrade in adverse weather. We address this challenge by integrating 4D imaging radar as a weather-robust modality into collaborative perception and introducing a Doppler-guided spatial attention mechanism for multi-agent fusion. Our approach extends two representative backbones: a radar-camera pipeline where radar substitutes LiDAR, and a LiDAR-radar pipeline where radar complements LiDAR. To support evaluation, we release radar-augmented benchmarks, OPV2V-R and Adver-City-R, with physics-based LiDAR degradation. Experiments show strong robustness gains in fog and rain, including substantial improvements when radar replaces degraded LiDAR. Additional validation on MAN TruckScenes demonstrates transfer beyond simulation. Overall, our results highlight 4D imaging radar as a robust modality for all-weather collaborative perception. Dataset and code are available at: https://url.fzi.de/SlimComm.

</details>


### [45] [Detect Before You Leap: Mirage Detection in Vision-Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00435)
*Sayeed Shafayet Chowdhury,Md. Shaown Miah*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为TC-LIA的模型无关方法，用于在视觉语言模型（VLM）生成答案前检测是否存在幻觉（mirage）现象。该方法通过分析CLIP ViT-H/14编码器各层的图像补丁标记与问题嵌入之间的对齐轨迹，结合多种特征和集成策略，在多个领域和不同条件下实现了高达94.7%的三分类检测准确率，将幻觉率降至3%以下，显著优于基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 许多视觉语言模型在缺乏实际视觉证据的情况下仍会生成看似合理但不基于图像内容的回答，这种‘幻觉’现象在医疗和文档问答等高风险场景中尤为危险，因此需要在回答前识别并避免此类错误输出。

Method: 提出Text-Conditioned Layer-wise Internal Alignment（TC-LIA），通过将各层图像补丁标记投影到最终的CLIP嵌入空间，并计算其与问题嵌入的相似性，追踪问题相关视觉证据在不同层次上的出现情况；结合最终图像-文本余弦相似度、晚期层top-k补丁-文本对齐、早期到晚期增益、层间斜率等特征，融合像素统计、零样本域路由和结构化自评估构成集成系统。

Result: 在五个VQA领域、三种输入条件和十二个VLM骨干网络上，最佳系统达到约94.6%-94.7%的三分类检测准确率，幻觉率低于3%，而基线幻觉率在21.7%至66.6%之间。

Conclusion: TC-LIA是一种有效且通用的预发布幻觉检测方法，能够可靠地识别VLM在无视觉依据时的错误自信输出，提升模型在关键应用中的可信度与安全性。

Abstract: Vision-language models (VLMs) can produce confident visual answers even when the required visual evidence is missing, blank, or unrelated to the question. This failure mode, known as mirage (Asadi et al. 2026), is especially concerning in medical and document visual question answering, where plausible but visually ungrounded responses may be mistaken for image-based evidence. We study pre-release mirage detection: given an image-question pair, the goal is to determine whether a VLM should answer or abstain before producing a response. We propose Text-Conditioned Layer-wise Internal Alignment (TC-LIA), a model-agnostic method that probes patch-token representations across the layers of a CLIP ViT-H/14 vision encoder. TC-LIA projects layer-wise image patch tokens into the final CLIP embedding space and measures their similarity to the question embedding, allowing the method to track whether question-relevant visual evidence emerges across vision layers. The resulting alignment trajectory is summarized using final image-text cosine similarity, late-layer top-k patch-text alignment, early-to-late gain, and layer-wise slope. These features are combined with pixel-statistic blank/noise detection, zero-shot domain routing, and structured VLM self-assessment in an ensemble. Across five VQA domains, three input conditions, and twelve VLM backbones, the best systems achieve approximately 94.6-94.7% three-class detection accuracy with mirage rates below 3%, while baseline mirage rates range from 21.7% to 66.6%.

</details>

Method: 构建DraDDP数据集，包含多模态（文本、音频、视频）对话数据；建立多任务评估框架，分析不同模态对对话话语结构识别的影响。

Abstract: Multi-party dialogue discourse parsing aims to identify dependency structures and relation types between utterances in conversations. Previous studies are mostly limited to textual modality or two-party dialogue, failing to meet the multimodal and multi-party settings. In this paper, we construct the first publicly available English multimodal dataset DraDDP for multi-party dialogue discourse parsing, based on American TV dramas. DraDDP contains 495 dialogue segments with 6,374 utterances and 9.1 hours of parallel video content, covering rich multi-party interaction scenarios. Moreover, we establish comprehensive benchmarks by evaluating this task on DraDDP and conducting in-depth analysis on the impact of different modalities. Experimental results demonstrate the value of multimodal information in capturing dialogue structures and relation types. We will publicly release the dataset, annotation guidelines, and code to promote future research in multimodal dialogue understanding.

### [47] [Toward Robust In-Context Learning: Leveraging Out-of-distribution Proxies for Target Inaccessible Demonstration Retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00014)
*Hao Xu,Rite Bo,Fausto Giunchiglia,Yingji Li,Rui Song*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出DOPA框架，通过引入OOD代理来近似不可访问的目标域，并指导演示检索，结合马哈拉诺比斯距离的全局多样性约束，提升LLMs在分布外任务中的鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究发现大语言模型在分布外任务上表现良好，但当分布偏移加剧时优势减弱；在目标域不可访问的情况下，评估未知分布困难，影响演示选择质量，因此需要一种有效的方法来检索分布相似且信息丰富的演示。

Method: DOPA框架利用OOD代理近似不可访问的目标域，指导演示检索过程，并引入基于马哈拉诺比斯距离的全局多样性约束，以确保所选演示的多样性。

Result: 在多个大语言模型和任务上的实验结果表明，DOPA能有效提升模型在分布外设置下的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: DOPA通过代理评估与多样性约束相结合，显著增强了大语言模型在严重分布偏移场景下的推理能力。

Abstract: Although studies have demonstrated that Large Language Models (LLMs) can perform well on Out-of-Distribution (OOD) tasks, their advantage tends to diminish as the distribution shift becomes more severe. Consequently, researchers aim to retrieve distributionally similar and informative demonstrations from the available source domain to boost the inference capabilities of LLMs. However, in practical scenarios where the target domain is inaccessible, evaluating the unknown distribution is challenging, which indirectly impacts the quality of the selected demonstrations. To address this problem, we propose \textbf{DOPA}, a demonstration search framework that incorporates an OOD proxy to approximate the inaccessible target domain and guide the retrieval process. Building on proxy-based evaluation, DOPA further introduces a Mahalanobis distance-based global diversity constraint to ensure sufficient diversity among the retrieved demonstrations. Experimental results on multiple LLMs and tasks demonstrate that DOPA effectively enhances robustness in OOD settings\footnote{https://github.com/bort64/ood\_code}.

### [48] [AEyeDE: An Attention-Based Attribution Framework for AI-Generated Text Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00016)
*Aria Nourbakhsh,Adelaide Danilov,Christoph Schommer,Salima Lamsiyah*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出AEyeDE方法，利用模型注意力作为判别信号进行人机文本生成检测。通过代理Transformer模型提取注意力归因矩阵，并用轻量CNN学习其表示，在编码器-解码器和解码器-only场景下均表现优异，且对跨数据集迁移和拼写扰动具有鲁棒性。注意力图中存在可区分的局部结构模式，为检测提供可解释的补充信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有检测方法依赖表面统计或似然信号，难以应对接近人类水平的AI生成文本。需要更深层、更具判别力的信号来区分人类与AI文本。

Method: 使用白盒访问的代理Transformer模型提取人类与AI生成文本的注意力归因矩阵，并训练轻量级CNN从这些归因图中学习特征表示，实现作者身份检测。

Result: 在编码器-解码器设置中优于纯文本基线；在解码器-only设置中表现出色，具备生成器特定检测能力，且在标准基准上保持竞争力，对跨数据集迁移和替代拼写扰动具有鲁棒性。注意力图中的局部结构频率差异稳定，可作为有效判别信号。

Conclusion: 注意力归因图提供了可解释且互补的人机生成文本判别信号，有助于提升检测性能，推动未来研究发展。

Abstract: Detecting AI-generated text is becoming increasingly challenging as modern language models approach human-level fluency and can evade detectors that rely on surface statistics or likelihood-based signals. We propose \textsc{AEyeDE}, an attribution-driven approach to human-AI authorship detection that leverages model attention as a discriminative signal. Specifically, we extract attention-based attribution matrices for both human- and AI-generated text using a \emph{proxy} Transformer model with white-box access and train a lightweight Convolutional Neural Network to learn representations from these attribution maps. Across encoder-decoder translation settings, our method consistently outperforms a text-only baseline. In decoder-only settings, it performs strongly in generator-specific detection, remains competitive on standard benchmarks, and shows robustness under cross-dataset transfer and alternative-spelling perturbations. We further show that attention maps exhibit recurring local structures whose relative frequencies differ consistently between human- and AI-generated text across datasets and proxy models. These findings suggest that attention-based attribution maps provide a complementary and interpretable signal for AI-generated text detection. We will make the code publicly available to support future research.

</details>


### [49] [CSRP: Chain-of-Thought Reasoning for Chinese Text Correction via Reinforcement Learning with Efficiency-Aware Rewards](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00020)
*Wei Tian,Yuhao Zhou,Man Lan*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出CSRP框架，通过持续预训练、思维链微调和基于效率感知奖励的相对策略优化，解决大语言模型在中文语法纠错中的领域知识不足与过度修正问题，在NACGEC和CSCD数据集上均取得领先性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于大语言模型的中文语法纠错系统存在缺乏领域语言先验知识以及监督微调导致过度修正的问题，影响纠错精度。

Method: 提出三阶段框架CSRP：1）在590万平衡样本上进行持续预训练以吸收领域知识；2）采用思维链监督微调实现错误推理的可解释性；3）使用新型效率感知奖励进行组相对策略优化，惩罚不必要的修改。

Result: 在NACGEC基准上达到50.99 $F_{0.5}$ 和 57.17 精度，显著优于之前最佳结果；在CSCD拼写纠错任务上达到59.61 F1，超过GPT-4 5.20点；消融实验表明强化学习对齐阶段带来8%相对提升，且与大规模持续预训练贡献正交。

Conclusion: 显式优化编辑效率对高质量语法纠错至关重要，所提方法有效缓解了最大似然估计带来的过度修正偏差，实现了更精准、可解释的中文语法纠错。

Abstract: Large Language Model (LLM) based Chinese Grammatical Error Correction (CGEC) systems face two critical challenges: general-purpose models lack specialized linguistic priors for subtle grammatical distinctions, and Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) with Maximum Likelihood Estimation fails to optimize for precision-focused metrics, leading to systematic over-correction. We propose CSRP, a three-stage framework that progressively builds correction capability through Continual Pre-training (CPT) on 5.9M balanced samples to internalize domain knowledge, Chain-of-Thought SFT with explicit error reasoning for diagnostic transparency, and Group Relative Policy Optimization with a novel Efficiency-Aware Reward that explicitly penalizes unnecessary edits. On the NACGEC benchmark, CSRP achieves state-of-the-art performance with 50.99 $F_{0.5}$ and 57.17 precision, substantially outperforming previous best results while effectively mitigating the over-correction bias inherent in MLE-trained models. Our method also advances CSCD spelling correction to 59.61 F1, surpassing GPT-4 by 5.20 points. Comprehensive ablation studies demonstrate that the RL alignment stage contributes a 8\% relative gain over the SFT baseline, and that this gain is orthogonal to the contribution of large-scale CPT, validating that explicit optimization for edit efficiency is essential for high-quality grammatical error correction. Our code is available at https://github.com/TW-NLP/ChineseErrorCorrector.

</details>


### [50] [SENSE: Semantic Embedding Navigation with Soft-gated Evaluation for Retrieval-based Speculative Decoding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00021)
*Shaowen Chen,Zhicheng Liao,Hongwei Wang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: SENSE提出一种基于语义嵌入导航的软门控评估方法，通过目标模型隐藏状态实现稳健的语义对齐，使验证模块关注语义等价性而非表面形式，从而克服传统检索式推测解码中因词汇依赖导致的脆弱性。在多个领域和模型（LLaMA、Qwen）上实验表明，SENSE可实现最高4.09的平均接受长度和3.26倍加速，同时保持生成质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有检索式推测解码（RSD）受限于刚性的词汇依赖，对表面形式变化敏感，导致检索与验证过程不稳定，影响性能和鲁棒性。

Method: SENSE通过将检索锚定在目标模型的隐藏状态上，建立更强的语义对齐；引入软门控评估模块，判断候选输出是否在语义层面等价于目标输出，而非仅匹配表面词形。

Result: 在多个数据集和模型（包括LLaMA和Qwen）上的实验显示，SENSE实现了最高4.09的平均接受长度和3.26倍推理加速，且生成质量未下降。

Conclusion: SENSE有效缓解了传统RSD对表面形式的依赖问题，通过语义对齐与软门控评估显著提升推测解码的效率与鲁棒性，为高效大模型推理提供了新范式。

Abstract: Speculative Decoding (SD) accelerates Large Language Model (LLM) inference by employing a lightweight draft model to propose candidate tokens, which are verified in parallel by the target model, without compromising generation quality. While Retrieval-based Speculative Decoding (RSD) is favored for its plug-and-play versatility, its potential is impeded by rigid lexical dependencies, rendering both retrieval and verification brittle to surface-level variations. To address this, we propose SENSE (Semantic Embedding Navigation with Soft-gated Evaluation). By anchoring retrieval on the hidden states of the target model, SENSE establishes robust semantic alignment, which empowers the Soft-gated Evaluation module to validate semantic equivalence rather than surface forms. To ensure rigorous benchmarking, we deconstruct existing methods into atomic primitives within a unified framework, facilitating granular, component-level comparison. Extensive experiments across diverse domains demonstrate that SENSE outperforms multiple baselines on the LLaMA and Qwen families, attaining up to 4.09 mean acceptance length and 3.26x speedup, while preserving generation quality. Our code will be released upon publication.

</details>


### [51] [lmfaoooo at SemEval-2026 Task 1: Humor Is an Audience. Preference Modeling for Constrained Humor Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00022)
*Alexey Tikhonov,Alexey Ivanov*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本论文针对幽默生成任务中的观众依赖性和标注噪声问题，提出了一种‘生成多候选 -> 选最佳’的策略。通过多步提示、模型集成和多样性解码生成多样化候选句，再利用基于人类对比判断训练的偏好模型筛选最优幽默输出。研究还发布了2.5K条人工成对判断数据，并构建可解释的偏好建模流程。系统在SemEval-2026任务中英语和中文子任务中排名第一，西班牙语子任务排名第二。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 幽默生成面临的主要挑战在于‘有趣’具有高度主观性，受受众、语境和文化影响，且人工标注的准确性低，导致监督信号噪声大。因此需要一种能适应多样偏好并有效利用有限高质量标注的方法。

Method: 采用‘生成多候选 -> 选最佳’框架：首先通过多步提示、模型集成与多样性解码生成大量候选幽默句；其次构建基于人类对比判断的偏好模型，以模拟读者偏好；最后用该模型对候选句进行排序，并发布候选池和排名结果供后续研究使用。

Result: 所提方法在三个偏好数据集上均优于基线模型，具备更强的跨域迁移能力；在SemEval-2026 MWAHAHA任务中，英文和中文子任务获得第一，西班牙语子任务获得第二。

Conclusion: 该系统通过结合多样性生成与基于人类偏好的选择机制，有效应对了幽默生成中的主观性与标注噪声问题，为多语言幽默生成提供了可复现、可解释的解决方案。

Abstract: Humor generation remains difficult not only because producing fluent, novel jokes is hard, but because "funny" is audience-dependent and supervision is noisy -- preferences vary with audience, context, and culture, and annotator agreement is often low. In this paper, we describe our system for the SemEval-2026 Task-1 (MWAHAHA), which focuses on humor generation under explicit constraints. The task evaluates submitted systems via human preference judgments in 1-on-1 arena-style comparisons.
  We adopt a "generate-many -> select-best" strategy. First, we generate a diverse pool of candidates per instance using multi-step prompting, model ensembling, and diversity-oriented decoding. Second, we select outputs using a preference model that approximates a "reader" by learning from human comparisons rather than absolute funniness scores. To support this approach, we release 2.5K human pairwise judgments collected through the Humor Arena prototype. We further propose an interpretable pipeline that converts labeled comparisons into a preference model. Across three preference datasets, our models consistently outperform baselines and show stronger cross-domain transfer. Finally, we apply the learned preference model to rank candidates for the MWAHAHA setting and release intermediate artifacts (candidate pools and rankings) to facilitate follow-up work.
  Our system ranked 1st in the English and Chinese subtasks of MWAHAHA and 2nd in the Spanish subtask.

</details>


### [52] [TrustLDM: Benchmarking Trustworthiness in Language Diffusion Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00023)
*Yichuan Mo,Yukun Jiang,Yanbo Shi,Mingjie Li,Michael Backes,Yang Zhang,Yisen Wang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究针对语言扩散模型（LDMs）的可信性问题，提出一个专门的基准测试TrustLDM，评估其在安全、隐私和公平性方面的表现。结果显示，当引入恶意后置上下文时，LDMs的对齐行为显著下降，且生成长度与解码顺序会影响结果。研究还提出了TrustLDM-Auto自动评估框架，系统识别出多种模型在不同配置下的可信性弱点，有助于提升LDMs的整体可信度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 语言扩散模型（LDMs）虽具备快速解码优势，但其非自回归的任意顺序生成机制可能带来新的可信性风险，亟需系统评估其在真实场景中的安全性、隐私性和公平性表现。

Method: 构建面向LDMs的可信性基准TrustLDM，涵盖多种静态后置上下文类型；通过实验分析不同上下文长度、解码顺序和生成长度对模型行为的影响；设计TrustLDM-Auto自动化评估框架，利用LDM的解码灵活性探测脆弱配置。

Result: LDMs在仅使用用户提示时表现良好，但在添加恶意后置上下文后对齐性能明显下降；上下文长度并非决定因素，解码顺序与生成长度显著影响评估结果；所有被测模型均暴露可信性弱点，证实了系统性风险的存在。

Conclusion: 本研究揭示了语言扩散模型在复杂上下文下的可信性隐患，提出有效的评估工具与方法，为构建更可信的LDMs提供了重要支持。

Abstract: The rapid development of Language Diffusion Models (LDMs) challenges the dominant position of auto-regressive competitors in language processing. However, their flexible, any-order decoding strategies not only enable fast decoding speed but also potentially bring new trustworthiness challenges. To better understand the risks behind their pipelines, we introduce a comprehensive trustworthiness benchmark tailored to LDMs (TrustLDM), evaluating safety, privacy, and fairness across different LDM architectures with multiple categories of static post contexts. Our empirical results show that although LDMs generally exhibit strong trustworthiness with only the user prompts, their alignment behavior degrades noticeably when the malicious post contexts are attached to the masked responses. We further observe that longer contexts do not necessarily induce stronger effects, and both decoding order and generation length affect the evaluation outcomes. Finally, we propose TrustLDM-Auto, an automatic evaluation framework that leverages LDM decoding flexibility to systematically identify vulnerable configurations, revealing substantial trustworthiness weaknesses across all evaluated models and dimensions. Our work may potentially help the community build more trustworthy LDMs. Our code is available at https://github.com/PKU-ML/TrustLDM.

</details>


### [53] [ART: Attention Run-time Termination for Efficient Large Language Model Decoding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00024)
*Chen Qiu,Guozhong Li,Panos Kalnis*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为ART的轻量级运行时机制，通过跟踪注意力输出累积情况，在后续KV块访问贡献可忽略时终止，从而减少内存带宽压力。该方法与现有基于键的缓存管理方法正交，可无缝集成。在LongBench基准测试中，ART在大批次下比最先进基线提升20%生成吞吐量，且保持相近准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长上下文解码受制于获取大量键值（KV）缓存所需的内存带宽；现有方法多依赖仅基于键的剪枝，但忽略了值对注意力输出的影响，而将值纳入处理又带来高昂开销。

Method: 提出Attention Run-time Termination (ART)，在核函数执行过程中实时追踪注意力输出的累积，并在进一步贡献可忽略时提前终止对后续KV块的访问。

Result: 在LongBench基准测试中，ART在大批次场景下实现20%更高的生成吞吐量，同时保持与基线相当的准确性。

Conclusion: ART是一种高效、轻量的运行时机制，能有效缓解长上下文解码中的内存带宽瓶颈，且可与现有方法兼容，具有良好的实用价值。

Abstract: Long-context decoding in Large Language Models (LLMs) is severely constrained by the memory bandwidth required to fetch the extensive Key-Value (KV) cache. Most existing KV management methods rely on key-only pruning before decoding, despite the evidence that attention outputs depend jointly on keys and values, as incorporating values in their methods incurs prohibitive additional overhead. In this paper, we propose Attention Run-time Termination (ART), a lightweight run-time mechanism that tracks accumulated attention outputs during kernel execution and terminates subsequent KV block accesses once further contributions become negligible. This design makes ART orthogonal to existing key-based KV cache management methods, enabling seamless integration with them. Experiments on LongBench benchmarks show that ART achieves 20% higher generation throughput in large batch size than state-of-the-art baseline while maintaining comparable accuracy.

*Brian Van Steen*

Conclusion: 结合认知理论指导的语言特征与先进的预训练模型，能够有效提升抑郁文本的自动化检测精度，且增强了模型的可解释性，为未来心理健康监测系统的设计提供了新思路。

Conclusion: 仅依靠平均准确率无法反映模型在临床实践中的真实可靠性；性能波动和最坏情况下的失败表现更具临床意义；未来评估应采用融合自动化与临床专家监督的混合方法，以实现可信的安全性验证。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed across healthcare, yet existing benchmarks fail to capture model behavior under adversarial or ethically complex conditions common in clinical practice. Scenarios incorporated adversarial transformations, and responses were assessed using a seven-dimension rubric with LLM-assisted scoring and human-in-the-loop validation. Results revealed substantial performance variance, with mean scores ranging from 0.791 to 0.984. Critically, several high-performing systems produced complete failures in individual safety-critical scenarios, demonstrating that aggregate accuracy masks clinically meaningful risk. Equity-related tasks showed 10-20% error amplification with demographic modifications, and human reviewers identified clinically relevant failures missed by automated evaluation. Our findings demonstrate that performance variance and worst-case failures provide more clinically meaningful reliability indicators than mean accuracy alone, and that hybrid evaluation approaches combining automation with clinician oversight are essential for credible safety assessment.

Abstract: Retrieval-augmented generation systems struggle with temporal reasoning and evidence fusion when answering complex questions over historical criminal case narratives. ### [58] [Graph-Augmented Retrieval for Cross-Entity Financial Sentiment Analysis: A Comparative Study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00062)
*Rajan Bastakoti,Sagar Bhetwal,Nirajan Acharya,Gaurav Kumar Gupta*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究提出一种新型双跳图-检索增强生成（Graph-RAG）架构，对比传统向量基RAG在跨实体金融情感分析中的表现。基于59个股票实体和255篇科技新闻构建情感加权知识图谱，通过强度过滤的图遍历机制补充向量搜索无法捕捉的多实体关系。在100个带背景查询（30个直接，70个关系型）上评估，Graph-RAG在实体召回率上提升6.4%（p < 0.001），复杂多实体问题的答案相关性提升11.7%，关系型问题提升达16.1%；答案语义相似度几乎无损（+0.001），仅延迟均值增加22.6%，但延迟方差下降80%。消融实验揭示图遍历强度阈值存在倒U型关系，最优值为tau=0.5，优于默认值tau=0.7。研究揭示图增强检索中的精度-覆盖权衡，并为金融领域多实体RAG系统设计提供可操作指导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建情感加权知识图谱，利用强度过滤的图遍历（INFLUENCES边）增强密集检索，实现对关系证据的挖掘；通过多维度评估（语义相似度、实体召回、RAGAS指标、延迟基准、消融实验）比较Graph-RAG与向量基基线性能。

Result: Graph-RAG在实体召回率上显著提升6.4%（p < 0.001），关系型问题答案相关性提升11.7%（关系类达16.1%），语义相似度几乎不变（delta = +0.001），延迟均值上升22.6%但方差下降80%；最优图遍历阈值为tau=0.5，低于生产默认值0.7。

Conclusion: 图增强检索在多实体金融分析中能有效提升关系推理能力，但需权衡精度与覆盖范围；建议采用tau=0.5作为优化阈值，为实际系统部署提供明确指导。

Abstract: Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) has become foundational for grounding large language models in domain-specific corpora, yet conventional vector-based RAG systems are fundamentally limited in their ability to capture the structured, multi-entity relationships that underpin financial market analysis. This paper presents a comprehensive comparative study of a novel two-hop Graph-RAG architecture versus a standard vector-only baseline for cross-entity financial sentiment analysis. Our system constructs a sentiment-weighted knowledge graph of 59 equity entities from 255 news articles covering 10 major technology stocks, then augments dense retrieval with intensity-filtered graph traversal over INFLUENCES edges to surface relational evidence inaccessible to vector search alone.
  We evaluate both architectures on 100 grounded queries (30 Direct, 70 Relational) using semantic similarity, entity recall, RAGAS metrics, latency benchmarks, and ablation studies. Graph-RAG achieves a statistically significant improvement in entity recall (+6.4%, p < 0.001, Wilcoxon signed-rank) and delivers substantially more relevant answers for complex multi-entity queries (+11.7% Answer Relevancy), with gains concentrating in relational question types (+16.1%). Critically, these improvements come at no measurable cost to answer quality (delta = +0.001 semantic similarity, Cohen's d = 0.078), with a modest 22.6% increase in mean latency offset by an 80% reduction in latency variance.
  An ablation study on the graph traversal intensity threshold reveals an inverted-U relationship with answer quality, identifying tau = 0.5 as optimal over the production default of tau = 0.7. These findings characterize a precision-for-coverage trade-off inherent to graph-augmented retrieval and provide actionable architectural guidance for practitioners building RAG systems for multi-entity financial analysis.

### [59] [DLLM-JEPA: Joint Embedding Predictive Architectures for Masked Diffusion Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00091)
*Sangdae Nam*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: DLLM-JEPA结合JEPA与掩码扩散语言模型，消除了自监督学习中对显式多视图数据和双前向传播的依赖，仅需单次梯度传播，训练计算量减少33%。在多个任务和架构上均优于纯扩散模型微调，提升显著（如LLaDA-8B GSM8K达+18.7 pp），并表现出双重优势：在提升下游任务准确率的同时降低外部文本损失并保持MMLU性能稳定。层间探查揭示了‘几何-功能漂移分离’机制，即微调后主干网络远离预训练权重但遗忘更少，且该现象在不同模型中具有一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自监督方法如LLM-JEPA依赖因果注意力结构，需显式多视图数据对及双前向传播，带来高计算开销；目标是设计一种无需显式配对、计算更高效的自监督框架。

Method: 将JEPA与掩码扩散语言模型结合，利用扩散模型的双向注意力生成不同掩码率下的语义差异视图，实现无需显式多视图数据的自监督训练，并通过单次前向传播完成梯度更新。

Result: 相比LLM-JEPA，训练FLOPs减少33%；在GSM8K、Spider、NL-RX-SYNTH、Django等任务上显著优于扩散模型微调；在LLaDA-8B Wide-t配置下，同时提升GSM8K准确率（+1.8 pp）、降低外部文本损失、维持MMLU准确率；层分析显示存在几何-功能漂移分离现象，主要集中在中间层。

Conclusion: DLLM-JEPA有效解决了传统JEPA在语言建模中的高成本问题，实现了更高效率与更强性能的统一，在多个基准上展现显著优势，其内在机制具有普适性，为自监督语言建模提供了新范式。

Abstract: Joint Embedding Predictive Architectures (JEPAs) have reshaped self-supervised representation learning in vision. The recent LLM-JEPA ported JEPA to autoregressive language models but inherited two steep costs from the causal-attention substrate: it demands explicit multi-view data (e.g., text-code pairs), and it requires two gradient-carrying forward passes per step. We introduce DLLM-JEPA, which pairs JEPA with masked-diffusion language models to eliminate both costs at once. The bidirectional attention of diffusion models yields two semantically distinct views of the same input via different masking rates -- no explicit pairs needed -- and supports a single gradient-carrying forward pass, cutting training FLOPs by 33% relative to LLM-JEPA. DLLM-JEPA improves over diffusion-only fine-tuning in every (task, architecture) combination we evaluate: up to +18.7 pp on LLaDA-8B GSM8K and +11.4 pp on Dream-7B GSM8K, with consistent positive gains on Spider, NL-RX-SYNTH, and Django. Beyond accuracy, DLLM-JEPA exhibits a dual-win property: on LLaDA-8B with the Wide-t configuration, it simultaneously raises GSM8K accuracy (67.1 vs. 65.2, +1.8 pp), drives held-out Wikitext loss below the pre-trained base, and preserves MMLU accuracy at base level across three fine-tuning seeds -- whereas an L2-to-base parameter anchor matches baseline accuracy with no task gain. Layer-wise probing reveals the mechanism: a geometric-functional drift dissociation in which the fine-tuned backbone moves further from the pre-trained weights than the baseline yet forgets less on held-out Wikitext, with the amplification concentrated in middle transformer layers. The pattern appears on Dream-7B as well, indicating the phenomenon is not specific to a single backbone.

</details>


### [60] [Agreement Metrics for LLM-as-Judge Evaluation: What to Report and Why](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00093)
*Delip Rao,Chris Callison-Burch*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文指出，在验证大语言模型（LLM）作为评判者时，多数研究报告的评估指标如准确率、精确率、召回率、F1分数、Cohen's κ以及各种秩相关系数在二元标准下存在冗余。对于二元评判（如是否满足标准），多种相关系数实际上等价于同一数值，因此报告多个指标只会制造出虚假的证据支持感。唯一提供额外信息的是Cohen's κ，因为它与phi系数共享分子但归一化方式不同，二者之差反映了模型正类判定率与人类标注者的偏离程度。当引入‘无法评估’（CANNOT_ASSESS）的拒绝选项时，三种常见处理方式并非可互换的预处理选择，而是回答了不同的问题，并破坏了原有的等价关系。这些等价性在多评判者集成评分中，使用Fleiss' κ或Krippendorff's α时依然成立，仅需微小的有限样本修正。文章最后提出一份报告清单，要求明确判断尺度、拒答与平局处理方式、覆盖率、混淆矩阵及聚合层级，并附带任意标量一致性系数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大多数使用大语言模型作为评判者的论文在评估其表现时，依赖多种看似多样实则冗余的统计指标，且对判断尺度、平局处理、无效输出和拒答处理等关键设定缺乏透明度。这种不一致和模糊性导致结果难以比较，也容易误导读者认为多个指标提供了多重验证，而实际上它们可能只是同一信息的不同表达。因此需要澄清哪些指标真正有效，如何正确解释和报告结果。

Method: 通过数学推导分析二元评判数据下各类一致性度量（如Pearson r、Spearman ρ、Kendall τ_b、phi系数φ、Matthews CC、Cohen's κ）之间的代数等价性；进一步探讨当引入‘无法评估’（CANNOT_ASSESS）类别时，三种典型处理方法（排除、视为错误、视为缺失）所对应的不同统计含义；并扩展到多评判者场景中的Fleiss' κ和Krippendorff's α，验证等价性在高阶聚合下的稳健性。

Result: 在非退化的二元评判数据中，除Cohen's κ外，其他所有相关系数均等价于同一数值，因此报告多个属于冗余。Cohen's κ提供额外信息，其与phi系数的差异揭示了模型正类预测频率与人类标注者的偏差。当存在拒答情况时，不同处理方式影响结果解释，不可互换。多评判者场景中，类似等价关系在有限样本修正下仍成立。

Conclusion: 为提升评估的透明性与科学性，应避免报告多个等价指标，优先报告Cohen's κ，并在报告中明确说明判断尺度、拒答与平局处理方式、覆盖率、混淆矩阵及聚合层级，以形成标准化的报告规范。

Abstract: Validating an LLM judge against human annotations usually means reporting several agreement statistics: accuracy, precision, recall, $F_1$, Cohen's $κ$, and one or more rank correlations. A survey of 24 recent LLM-as-judge papers finds metric choice entangled with the judgment scale, tie handling, invalid outputs, and abstention handling, and those choices rarely stated. For binary criteria -- the common case in rubric-based evaluation, where each criterion is graded MET or UNMET -- most of the reported numbers are redundant: Pearson's $r$, Spearman's $ρ$, Kendall's $τ_b$, the phi coefficient $φ$, and the Matthews Correlation Coefficient all reduce to a single number on non-degenerate binary data, so reporting several of them only creates an illusion of corroborating evidence. Cohen's $κ$ is the one agreement coefficient that adds information: it shares $φ$'s numerator but normalizes differently, and the gap between them measures how far the judge's positive-label rate has drifted from the human's. We then trace what changes when a judge may abstain with a CANNOT_ASSESS verdict: the three common ways of handling abstentions are not interchangeable preprocessing choices but answer different questions, and they break the binary equivalences. The same equivalences reappear, up to a negligible finite-sample correction, for multi-judge ensembles scored with Fleiss' $κ$ or Krippendorff's $α$. We close with a reporting checklist that names the judgment scale, the abstention and tie handling mode, coverage, the confusion matrix, and the aggregation level alongside any scalar agreement coefficient.

</details>


### [61] [Enhancing BiGRU with a KAN Block for Legal Document Classification and Summarization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00116)
*Ahmed Faizul Haque Dhrubo,Souvik Pramanik,Most. Aysha Siddika Sumona,Shahnewaz Siddique,Mohammad Ashrafuzzaman Khan,Mohammad Abdul Qayum,Mohsin Sajjad*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究提出一种基于KAN的BiGRU模型，用于低资源多语言环境下的法律文档分类与摘要任务。针对领域语言差异、多语言使用、长距离依赖和类别不平衡等问题，采用来自孟加拉国和Manupatra的包含孟加拉语、英语及转写孟加拉语的法律文档数据集。分类部分结合了BiGRU与Kolmogorov-Arnold网络（KAN）模块，摘要部分则采用基于注意力机制的GRU结合KAN模型头。分类准确率达到67.96%，F1得分为0.65；摘要的ROUGE-1、ROUGE-2和ROUGE-L得分分别为0.38、0.23和0.31。消融实验表明，引入KAN使分类准确率从57.34%提升至67.96%。与多种基线方法（包括传统机器学习算法和预训练语言模型）相比，所提方法表现更优。

Conclusion: 所提出的KAN-BiGRU模型在低资源多语言法律文本处理任务中表现出色，有效缓解了语言多样性与数据不平衡带来的挑战，优于多种基线方法。

Abstract: This study introduces a novel architecture of KAN-based BiGRU model for the task of classification and summarization of legal documents in a low-resource multilingual setup. In order to tackle problems associated with domain language, the usage of different languages, long dependencies within context, and class imbalance, we employ the dataset composed of legal documents from Bangladesh and taken from Manupatra, which include Bengali, English, and transliterated Bengali languages. Our classification task involves BiGRU model, along with Kolmogorov-Arnold Network (KAN) module, while the summarization part utilizes attention-based GRU, combined with a KAN model head. Classification model yields 67.96% of accuracy and 0.65 F1 score; while ROUGE-1, ROUGE-2, and ROUGE-L measures for summarization yield 0.38, 0.23, and 0.31 F1 scores, correspondingly. Ablation study shows that the use of KAN increases classification accuracy from 57.34% to 67.96%. Moreover, our proposed technique is compared to several baselines, including classical ML algorithms and pretrained language models.

### [62] [RealityTest: How People Probe AI Identity and Whether Models Disclose It](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00168)
*Anna Gausen,Sarenne Wallbridge,Bessie O'Dell,Christopher Summerfield,Hannah Rose Kirk*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: RealityTest 是首个大规模多模态、多语言的 AI 识别披露评估基准，基于来自 49 个国家、五种语言、约 750 名参与者的真实人类数据，收集了 3,152 条身份探测问题。研究发现仅 31% 的人在模糊情境下直接询问身份，且人类提问方式远比机器生成的问题多样化。测试 17 个文本模型和 6 个语音模型后发现披露行为差异显著，但单一抑制指令可将披露率降至 30% 以下。研究强调提问方式与对话上下文比模型本身对披露行为影响更大，提示现有基于狭窄或合成查询集的安全评估可能误判真实场景中的模型表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前 AI 系统在对话场景中普遍存在用户难以判断其是否为人工智能的问题，而现有评估多局限于英文、机器生成问题和纯文本，缺乏真实世界多样性与多模态支持，导致安全评估可能失真。因此亟需更贴近现实的评估方法。

Method: 构建 RealityTest 基准，基于真实人类在 49 个国家、五种语言中收集的 3,152 条身份探测问题（含文本与语音），涵盖真实对话情境；测试 17 个文本模型和 6 个语音模型的披露行为，并分析提问方式、上下文与模型类型的影响。

Result: 仅 31% 的人会在模糊情境中直接询问身份；人类提问形式多样，远超机器生成；不同模型披露行为差异大；但加入抑制指令后，所有模型披露率均低于 30%；提问方式与对话上下文对披露影响大于模型本身。

Conclusion: 现有基于合成或窄范围查询的安全评估无法准确反映真实场景中 AI 模型的披露行为。必须采用多样化、人类驱动的评估数据以提升安全性评估的有效性与真实性。

Abstract: AI systems are increasingly deployed in conversational settings where users may be uncertain whether they are speaking with a human or an AI. Despite mounting regulatory attention to this known safety risk, existing evaluations of AI disclosure are typically English-only, based on machine-generated questions, and restricted to text. We present RealityTest to comprehensively test whether AI systems disclose their identity when asked. The benchmark is the first large-scale multimodal and multilingual evaluation, grounded in human data on how people actually encounter and question AI identity in the real-world. Alongside the benchmark, we release the underlying dataset of 3,152 identity-probing queries collected from ~750 participants across 49 countries and five languages, in text and speech scenarios. We find that only 31% of people ask about identity directly in ambiguous scenarios, and that the questions people ask are far more diverse than machine-generated queries. We test 17 text and 6 speech models, and find substantial variation in disclosure behaviour. However, a single suppression instruction reduces disclosure rates to below 30%, even in the best-performing models. Validating our investment in diverse, human-grounded evaluation data, we find that how the question is phrased and the context of the conversation matter more for disclosure than which model is being tested. Safety evaluations built on narrow or synthetic query sets risk mischaracterising how models behave in realistic deployment settings.

Abstract: The rapid spread of fake news on social media has become a major challenge, particularly in multilingual and under-resourced contexts such as North Africa. In this paper, we introduce BOUTEF, a large-scale multilingual corpus designed to study the propagation, characteristics, and impact of fake news in Algeria and Tunisia. The corpus integrates three complementary components: fake narratives, genuine narratives, and associated user-generated comments, along with verified debunking information. It covers a wide range of languages and linguistic varieties, including MSA, Algerian and Tunisian dialects, Arabizi, French, English, and code-switched language. Building on this resource, we conduct a comprehensive empirical analysis combining quantitative and qualitative approaches. We examine thematic distributions, linguistic and rhetorical strategies, sentiment patterns, and social engagement dynamics. Statistical analyses reveal significant associations between thematic categories and message veracity, as well as strong correlations between user engagement and the visibility of fake content. Our findings show that fake news relies heavily on emotionally charged narratives, sensational framing, and hybrid linguistic practices that enhance virality and audience engagement. In contrast, debunking content adopts a more factual and verification-oriented style. Furthermore, a comparative analysis between Algeria and Tunisia highlights both shared dynamics and country-specific characteristics shaped by sociopolitical contexts. The results emphasize the role of informal language practices in the diffusion and reception of misinformation. By providing a rich, annotated, and publicly available dataset, this work contributes to advancing research on fake news detection, low-resource language processing, and the understanding of information disorders in complex linguistic environments.

### [64] [DeSQ: Decomposition-based SPARQL Query Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00203)
*Papa Abdou Karim Karou Diallo,Aditya Sharma,Neshat Elhami Fard,Amal Zouaq*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: DeSQ 是一种基于分解的 SPARQL 查询生成框架，通过将复杂问题分解为原子约束（ACs），生成结构化输出（SPARQL 片段与实体绑定），并组装成完整查询，有效结合了生成式与检索式方法的优势。在五个主流基准中，有四个表现优于现有方法，且对词汇变化更具鲁棒性。此外，该框架无需实时知识库端点，简化评估，并支持细粒度错误分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 KBQA 方法存在两大局限：生成形式化查询易受干扰且可解释性差；直接通过知识库探索检索答案则计算成本高且易产生幻觉。因此需要一种兼具高效性、鲁棒性和可解释性的新方法。

Method: DeSQ 框架包含三个阶段：(1) 将复杂问题分解为原子约束（ACs）；(2) 生成两部分结构化输出：① 将每个 AC 映射到标准占位符的 SPARQL 片段；② 提供占位符对应的实体 URI 绑定；(3) 组装片段生成完整 SPARQL 查询。

Result: DeSQ 在五个主流基准中，有四个超越当前最优方法，在面对词汇变化时表现出更强的鲁棒性；同时无需依赖实时知识库，便于评估和错误定位，显著提升可维护性与可解释性。

Conclusion: DeSQ 通过结构化分解与生成策略，实现了高性能、高鲁棒性与高可解释性的统一，为 KBQA 提供了一种轻量、可扩展且易于分析的新范式。

Abstract: Dominant approaches to Knowledge Base Question Answering (KBQA) fall into two categories. First is the generation of a formal query that suffers from brittleness and limited explainability, and the second is direct answer retrieval through KB exploration that is computationally costly and prone to hallucination. To combine the strengths of both paradigms while mitigating their respective weaknesses, we introduce DeSQ (Decomposition-based SPARQL Query Generation), a KB-agnostic framework that operates in three stages. First, it decomposes complex questions into Atomic Constraints (ACs) that mirror the relational structure of the underlying KB. Second, it generates a two-part structured output: (a) Mapping of each AC to its corresponding SPARQL Fragment, using standardized variable and URIs placeholders, and (b) URIs Grounding block describing each placeholder. Third, it assembles these fragments into a complete SPARQL query. DeSQ surpasses state-of-the-art approaches on four out of five major benchmarks and demonstrates superior robustness to lexical variation. Beyond performance gains, our framework greatly simplifies evaluation by eliminating the need for a live KB endpoint, and its structured output enables fine-grained error analysis, allowing more targeted interventions for improvement.

</details>


### [65] [Effects of Varying LLM Access on Essay Writing Behavior](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00250)
*Julia Christenson,Karin de Langis,Shirley Anugrah Hayati,Dongyeop Kang*

Main category: cs.CL

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究大语言模型在高等教育中对学生写作表现、参与度及作者认同感的影响，以制定既能支持学习又能避免削弱学生自主性的整合策略。

Method: 开展一项随机对照试点研究，将24名大学生分为三组：无LLM访问、有限访问（≤3次提示，响应≤100词）、无限访问，比较其写作表现、行为模式及主观感受。

Result: 三组作文质量无统计学差异；有限访问组学生报告更高的作者归属感、更强的组织能力提升，且提问更具策略性和修订导向；无限访问组耗时更长，文章更像AI生成，自我创造力感知下降。

Conclusion: 适度约束大语言模型的使用，而非全面禁止，可能在保持AI辅助价值的同时，有效维护学生的作者身份认同与学习主动性。

Abstract: Investigating the degree to which large language models (LLMs) affect teaching and learning in universities can help identify strategies for integrating LLMs in a way that supports, rather than undermines, student learning outcomes. This study examined how varying levels of LLM assistance affect writing performance, engagement, and perceived authorship. We report a pilot study in which 24 college students were randomly assigned to write a short essay with no LLM access, limited access (<=3 prompts, responses capped at 100 words), or unlimited access. Overall essay quality was statistically indistinguishable across groups. Yet writing behavior and perceived authorship diverged sharply: students with limited access reported higher ownership (62.5% would submit the essay as independent work, vs. 25% in the unlimited group), stronger organizational gains, and more strategic, revision-focused prompting. The unlimited group spent more time writing, produced essays more similar to LLM output, and reported reduced creative expression. Our findings suggest that constraining, rather than banning, LLM access may preserve authorship confidence while retaining the scaffolding benefits of AI assistance.

### [66] [Parameter Alignment Mitigates Catastrophic Forgetting in Multilingual Expert Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00284)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决多语言持续预训练中因微调导致的灾难性遗忘问题，特别是通用知识的丢失，提升模型在新语言学习与原有任务表现间的平衡。

Method: 提出五种分层参数对齐策略：硬层冻结、软正则化、事后权重恢复、模型融合，并系统比较其在多语言环境下的性能表现。

Result: 参数对齐显著减少遗忘，其中层冻结和正则化最有利于保持阅读理解能力，事后权重恢复在翻译任务上表现最佳；各策略可针对不同任务进行选择以优化性能。

Conclusion: 通过分层参数对齐，实现了家族专家型持续预训练中语言习得与知识保留的平衡，为实际部署提供了基于任务匹配的策略指导。

Abstract: While continual pretraining~(CPT) is a practical way to extend large language models to new languages, naïve finetuning on targeted data erodes existing capabilities through catastrophic forgetting. Organizing training around language families reduces cross-language interference but cannot alone prevent forgetting of the general knowledge needed for downstream tasks. We link this forgetting to parameter drift in multilingual CPT and present a suite of five layer-aware parameter alignment strategies: hard layer freezing, soft regularization, post-hoc weight reversion, and model merging. We systematically compare our alignment strategies against two unregularized CPT baselines on benchmarks spanning 32 training languages from five language families, plus held-out languages, across four evaluation axes: perplexity, reading comprehension, physical reasoning, and translation. Parameter alignment substantially reduces forgetting at minimal cost to language acquisition: layer freezing and regularization best preserve comprehension, whereas post-hoc reversion yields the strongest translation gains. Together, these results map the acquisition--forgetting frontier for family-expert CPT and offer practical deployment guidelines pairing each strategy to the tasks it best serves.

### [67] [Model-Based Quality Assessment for Massively Multilingual Parallel Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00285)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决大规模多语言双语数据中存在的非平行句对和低质量翻译问题，提升数据质量评估的准确性和适用性。

Method: 将模型评估分解为并行性评估（使用多语言嵌入模型）和无参考质量估计（QE），分别在FLORES-200和BOUQuET任务上进行基准测试，并评估多种评估器在不同语言对上的表现。

Result: 无模型在所有语言对上均表现稳定；简单集成削弱强信号；目标语言覆盖范围与高QE得分正相关；多语言平行数据评估需方向感知的路由与校准策略。

Abstract: Large-scale multilingual bitext often contains two distinct problems: non-parallel sentence pairs and low-quality translations. We decompose model-based assessment for such data into two independent components: parallelism assessment with multilingual embeddings and reference-free quality estimation (QE). For parallelism, we benchmark four embedding models on FLORES-200 and BOUQuET retrieval tasks, covering 6,654 source--target directions in our target language-pair inventory. For QE, we evaluate nine reference-free evaluators on professional FLORES-200 translations across 41,412 ordered source--target directions. Results show that no model is universally reliable across translation directions. Naive QE ensembles dilute strong model signals, while documented target-language coverage is strongly associated with higher QE scores. Overall, these findings suggest that multilingual parallel-data assessment is best approached as a direction-aware routing and calibration problem, where no single universal metric is expected to suffice across all languages.

In news discourse, references to the past, present, and future can function as rhetorical devices that shape interpretation and persuasion. Here, we study temporal framing, defined as the persuasive use of time-related language to structure meaning rather than to report chronology. We propose a taxonomy of eight temporal frames grounded in prior work on temporality and framing, and we realize it through expert annotation of a multilingual news corpus. ### [69] [Bridging Reasoning Trajectories in On-Policy Distillation via Near-Future Guidance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00305)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有On-Policy Distillation（OPD）虽采样自轨迹，但其学习信号局限于令牌级，无法可靠地将学生轨迹引导至教师轨迹，尤其在处理非实质性高损失令牌和分布漂移问题时表现不佳。

Method: 提出轨迹感知的On-Policy Distillation（TOPD），利用近未来轨迹信息识别真实分歧状态，并将指导信号分布到多个未来令牌，以克服局部修正的局限性。

Abstract: On-Policy Distillation (OPD) improves large language model reasoning by training a student model on trajectories sampled from its own policy under teacher supervision. Although OPD operates on trajectories, its learning signal remains token-level: it identifies deviations through high-loss tokens and repairs them through local reverse-KL correction. We show that this "trajectory-sampled but token-learned" mechanism cannot reliably bridge student trajectories toward teacher trajectories. About 30% of high-loss tokens fall into the low-divergence regime, indicating that many are surface-form mismatches rather than real reasoning forks. Moreover, even truly divergent tokens are difficult to repair with isolated token-level supervision, since reasoning failures often unfold as short-horizon distributional drift. We propose Trajectory-aware OPD (TOPD), which uses near-future trajectory information to identify real divergent states and distribute guidance across multiple future tokens. Experiments show that suppressing non-divergent high-loss tokens improves standard OPD from 47.8% to 48.2% average accuracy, while TOPD further improves performance to 52.2%, with gains on AIME24 from 60.0% to 63.3% and AIME25 from 46.7% to 53.3%.

### [70] [Which Institutional Frameworks Do Chatbots Assume? Auditing Jurisdictional Defaults in Multilingual LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00333)
*Zhizhi Wang,Harini Suresh*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了多语言大模型在未明确指定司法管辖区时，是否会将输入语言作为默认的管辖地信号。通过评估中美开发的七款大模型在中英文60个未指定管辖地的法律行政问题上的表现，发现中文输入更常产生中国相关答案，英文输入则更多指向美国或通用/比较性答案。当要求单一答案时，74.5%的英文输入响应采用美国框架，53.3%的中文输入采用中国框架。这种倾向在所有模型中均存在，作者称之为‘制度框架误选风险’，并建议接口不应仅根据输入语言提供制度建议，应在缺少位置信息时主动询问或声明答案的适用范围。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着大模型在税务、劳动保护、医疗、教育、养老和行政程序等领域的应用增多，其回答的准确性高度依赖于具体司法管辖区。然而，多语言用户常以母语提问，而非与目标地区相关的语言。因此，需探究大模型是否默认将输入语言视为管辖地信号，从而避免因语言与实际管辖地不一致导致错误指导。

Method: 对七款由美国或中国开发的大模型进行多语言审计，使用60个未指定司法管辖区的法律行政问题，在中英文双语下，结合三种系统提示条件，共生成2,520条人工标注的回答，分析不同输入语言下的管辖地选择倾向。

Result: 中文输入更倾向于输出中国相关法律行政框架，英文输入则更常输出美国相关、比较性或通用答案；当要求单一答案时，英文输入中74.5%采用美国框架，中文输入中53.3%采用中国框架，该趋势在所有模型中一致出现。

Conclusion: 大模型在缺乏明确地理位置信息时，会基于输入语言自动推断管辖地，可能导致制度框架误选。这可能误导用户，尤其当其语言偏好与实际适用法律区域不一致时。因此，大模型界面不应仅依据输入语言提供制度建议，而应在位置缺失时主动请求或说明答案的管辖范围。

Abstract: LLMs increasingly answer questions about taxes, labor protections, healthcare, education, pensions, and administrative procedures, where usefulness often depends on the applicable jurisdiction. Multilingual users may write in their most comfortable language rather than one associated with the country or region whose rules apply. We ask whether deployed LLMs use input language as a default jurisdictional signal when prompts omit any country or region. Prior multilingual audits show that prompt language can shift cultural, political, or normative outputs; we examine which legal-administrative framework models supply when jurisdiction is underspecified. We evaluate seven LLMs developed in the United States or China on 60 underspecified legal-administrative prompts in English and Mandarin Chinese under three system-prompt conditions, yielding 2,520 manually annotated responses. Across models and conditions, Chinese input more often produces China-specific answers, while English input more often produces U.S.-specific, comparative, or generic answers. Prompts requiring a single answer further increase jurisdiction selection: pooled across models, 74.5% of English-input responses adopt a U.S. framework, while 53.3% of Chinese-input responses adopt a China framework. This directional pattern appears in all seven models. We describe this deployment-level pattern as institutional-framework misselection risk: a fluent answer may rely on a legal-administrative context the user did not intend, especially when their preferred language differs from the relevant jurisdiction. LLM interfaces should not route institutional advice by input language alone; when location is absent, they should request it or state the jurisdictional scope of the answer.

Method: 提出三角化偏好转移得分，结合人类黄金标准、基础模型输出与指令微调模型输出，通过三重比较分离出偏好学习引起的特定行为变化。

Conclusion: 该方法为量化偏好学习引发的语言行为转变提供了首个自动化途径，有助于改进模型对齐策略，推动更可信的人工智能发展。

Abstract: Various language domains have undergone remarkable changes in recent years; these shifts are largely attributed to the advent of Large Language Models and their misalignment with natural language usage. These misalignments are thought to partly originate in the preference-learning stage, e.g. Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback, which generally makes models more useful but simultaneously may introduce systematic lexical bias. In terms of lexical behavior, this is visible in a model's preference for certain formats or the overuse of words (delve, furthermore), even when such patterns are not present in base model outputs. Research on lexical misalignment induced during preference training is constrained by reliance on manual curation. We address this, by introducing the Triangulated Preference Shift score, a metric that triangulates between human gold standards, base models, and instruct variants to isolate shifts induced specifically by preference learning, without manual curation. We provide data across six model families, anchor the results in the literature, and illustrate the general approach's utility by analyzing whether preference learning shifts models toward what could be interpreted as a "language of prestige". The metric provides an initial automated method to quantify behavioral shifts attributable to preference tuning, and thus, may help inform model alignment and development of trustworthy AI.

### [72] [How Far Do Auto-Interpretation Labels Generalize: A Controlled Study Across Languages, Scripts, and Rewordings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00356)
*Sripad Karne*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了稀疏自编码器（SAE）特征在不同语言和书写系统间的泛化能力，发现尽管跨语言的特征具有较高重叠度，但自动生成的自然语言标签在解释这些特征时表现不佳，尤其在塞尔维亚语的西里尔字母和拉丁字母之间差异显著，表明标签可能反映的是训练数据中常见输入的表现，而非概念本身。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用塞尔维亚语的双文字系统（拉丁与西里尔字母）作为受控实验环境，通过比较同一概念在不同书写形式下的SAE特征激活情况及自动标签的准确性，分析特征的跨语言一致性与标签的有效性。

Result: SAE特征在不同书写系统间有较高的重叠度（最高Jaccard相似度0.57），表明存在跨语言语义特征；但自动标签在解释塞尔维亚语中的特征时失败率比英语高4倍，且在西里尔字母上比拉丁字母更差，说明标签未能准确反映实际语义，且随着网络深度增加，差距扩大。

Conclusion: 自动生成的解释标签可能更多反映了特征在训练数据中常见输入上的行为，而非其所代表的概念本身，提示其在跨语言应用中存在局限性。

Abstract: Sparse autoencoder (SAE) features are increasingly used to interpret language models, with auto-generated natural-language labels serving as the primary interface for understanding what each feature represents. We ask whether these labels generalize: does a feature labeled for a concept actually track that concept across languages and scripts? Using Serbian digraphia as a controlled testbed -- the same language written in both Latin and Cyrillic via deterministic transliteration -- we first find that SAE feature sets activated by the same content in different languages, scripts, and wordings share substantial overlap (peak Jaccard similarity 0.57 vs.\ 0.13 random baseline), suggesting genuine cross-lingual semantic features. We then test whether auto-interpretation labels keep pace. They often do not: features whose labels describe semantic content miss the same meaning in Serbian up to $4\times$ more often than within English, and miss Serbian Cyrillic more than Serbian Latin -- two scripts that are deterministic transliterations of each other -- suggesting the failures track how well each form is represented in training. The gap grows with network depth, yet the labels give no indication that they fail. These results suggest that auto-interpretation labels may reflect a feature's behavior on well-represented inputs rather than the concept itself.

### [73] [Masking Stale Observations Helps Search Agents -- Until It Doesn't: A Regime Map and Its Mechanism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00408)
*Haoxiang Zhang,Qixin Xu,Zhuofeng Li,Lei Zhang,Pengcheng Jiang,Yu Zhang,Julian McAuley*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文研究了长时序搜索代理中观察值遮蔽对上下文效率的影响，发现其性能提升呈非对称倒U型曲线，受检索器召回率与模型隐式过滤能力的交互影响。遮蔽通过实现令牌与回合数之间的权衡，优化上下文使用，但过度遮蔽会损失关键证据。研究揭示了上下文管理应根据不同运行状态进行调整，并提供了可复现的研究框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长时序搜索代理在多轮工具调用中积累大量内容，导致上下文预算紧张，亟需有效的上下文管理策略。现有方法如遮蔽过时观察值虽简单，但其有效性机制尚不明确，缺乏系统性理解。

Method: 通过系统实验，考察4B至284B参数量级的多种模型骨干与三种检索器在离线和实时网络搜索基准上的表现，分析观察值遮蔽对准确率的影响，并结合机制分析揭示其背后的动态交互关系。

Result: 观察值遮蔽带来的准确率提升随模型能力变化呈现非对称倒U型曲线：弱检索器下无明显增益，强检索器搭配中等容量模型时达到峰值，而模型过饱和时则急剧下降。该现象源于检索器召回率与模型隐式过滤能力的协同作用。遮蔽通过释放上下文空间换取更多交互回合，仅在能将失败转为成功时有效；若移除模型本可能利用的关键证据，则反而造成性能下降。

Conclusion: 上下文管理并非通用策略，而应视系统运行状态而定。本文提出以‘状态依赖’视角重新理解上下文使用，强调需综合考虑检索质量与模型能力的匹配关系，为未来智能搜索系统设计提供新范式。并开源了实验框架与轨迹数据以支持后续研究。

Abstract: Long-horizon search agents accumulate large amounts of retrieved content across many tool calls, making context-budget efficiency increasingly important. A minimal intervention is to mask stale observations from the context as the trajectory progresses, but it remains unclear when this form of context management helps and why. We study observation masking through a systematic sweep over various agent backbones (4B to 284B parameters) and three retrievers on offline and live-web agentic search benchmarks. We find that the accuracy gain from masking follows an asymmetric inverted-U shape when plotted against the model's accuracy without context management: a plateau under weak retrievers, a peak when a strong retriever meets a mid-capacity model, and a sharp collapse when the model is saturated. This pattern reflects the interaction between retriever recall and the model's implicit filtering capacity, rather than either factor in isolation. Mechanistically, masking implements a token-for-turn trade-off: it removes observations the model has largely stopped attending to and pages the agent rarely re-opens. The added turns help when they convert failures into successes, but they fail when masking removes evidence the model would otherwise have used. We therefore reframe context management as a regime-dependent intervention and provide a holistic perspective for analyzing context use in agentic deep search. We release our scaffold and trajectories here (https://github.com/i-DeepSearch/observation-masking) to support future research.

</details>


### [74] [ProtStructQA: A Denotation Threshold in Protein Structural Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00451)
*Aravind Mandiga,Guoming Li,Jin Lu,Ismailcem Budak Arpinar,Khaled Rasheed,Samuel E. Aggrey*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出ProtStructQA，一个可执行的蛋白质结构问答基准，将自然语言问题转化为隐藏的领域特定语言（DSL）程序，并通过AlphaFold预测结构执行以获得答案。涵盖382.2K个问题，包括置信度、距离、预测对齐误差（PAE）、溶剂暴露、二级结构、拓扑和接触等维度，包含330K个活跃基准和52.2K个硬负样本鲁棒性池。评估Qwen3系列模型（0.6B至8B）在直接提示、思维链、语法约束可执行投票、带思维链的可执行投票及多轮ReAct式工具使用下的表现，发现1.7B与4B之间存在能力依赖的指称阈值：低于此阈值时，工具辅助的ReAct主导；高于时，思维链从有害转为显著有益，成为多数任务最强策略。解析失败与家族级分析表明该阈值是语言不可解析到可执行结构指称的转变点，而语法与执行在PAE和二级结构查询中仍具选择性价值。该基准重新定义科学问答为从语言到测量的编译过程，提供诊断测试平台以判断语言模型能否将词汇映射为可执行的三维结构测量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有蛋白质语言模型评估多依赖生成生物文本的合理性，但缺乏对精确结构语义（如三维坐标系中的测量）的严格检验。为填补这一空白，需要一种能将自然语言问题转化为可执行结构测量的基准，以更准确评估模型对蛋白质结构信息的理解与推理能力。

Method: 构建ProtStructQA基准，基于隐藏的类型化领域特定语言（DSL）程序生成自然语言问题，每个问题对应一个可执行的结构计算任务。使用AlphaFold预测的蛋白质结构作为输入，通过执行对应的DSL程序获取答案。数据集包含382.2K个问题，分为330K活跃基准和52.2K硬负样本池，覆盖多种结构属性。对Qwen3系列模型进行多种推理策略测试，包括直接提示、思维链、语法约束可执行投票、带思维链的可执行投票以及多轮ReAct式工具调用。

Result: 在未微调情况下，模型表现呈现明显的“能力阈值”现象：低于1.7B参数量时，工具辅助的ReAct策略最优；超过4B后，思维链从负面影响转变为强增益，成为多数任务中最优策略。解析失败分析显示该阈值标志着语言从无法解析到可生成可执行结构指称的转变。语法和执行机制在处理PAE和二级结构问题时仍具关键价值。

Conclusion: ProtStructQA将科学问答重构为语言到结构测量的编译过程，提供了诊断语言模型是否具备将自然语言映射为可执行三维结构测量能力的测试平台。研究揭示了模型能力与推理策略之间的非线性关系，为未来大模型在结构生物学中的应用提供了重要指导。

Abstract: Protein-language systems are often evaluated by whether they generate plausible biological text, but a structural question has a sharper semantics: it denotes a measurement in a 3D coordinate system. We introduce ProtStructQA, an executable benchmark for protein structural question answering in which each natural-language question is generated from a hidden typed domain-specific language (DSL) program and the answer is obtained by executing that program on an AlphaFold-predicted structure. ProtStructQA releases 382.2K questions covering confidence, distances, predicted aligned error (PAE), solvent exposure, secondary structure, topology and contacts, and held-out compositions: a 330K active benchmark over 10K proteins from four species, plus a 52.2K hard-negative robustness pool. Without fine-tuning, we evaluate Qwen3 models from 0.6B to 8B under direct prompting, chain-of-thought, grammar-constrained executable voting, executable voting with chain-of-thought, and multi-turn ReAct-style tool use, and replicate the headline finding on Gemma-3-1B and Gemma-3-12B. We find a capability-dependent denotation threshold between Qwen3-1.7B and Qwen3-4B: below it, tool-mediated ReAct dominates because models often fail to produce executable denotations; above it, chain-of-thought flips from mostly harmful to strongly beneficial and becomes the strongest strategy on most splits. Parse-failure and family-level analyses show that the threshold is a transition from unparseable language to executable structural denotation, while grammar and execution remain selectively valuable for PAE and secondary-structure queries. ProtStructQA reframes scientific QA as compilation from language to measurement and provides a diagnostic testbed for when language models can map words to executable 3D structural measurements.

</details>


### [75] [SALSA: Speech Aware LLM Adaptation via Learned Steering Activation Vectors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00460)
*Yekaterina Yegorova,Argyrios Gerogiannis,Haolong Zheng,Julia Hockenmaier,Chang D. Yoo,Mark A. Hasegawa-Johnson*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: SALSA是一种轻量级的语音感知大语言模型适应方法，通过学习层间导向向量来提升模型在跨领域语音任务中的表现。它不依赖对比激活差异，而是采用监督目标直接优化导向向量，在儿童语音、多语言语音和中英混用等基准上显著优于零样本推理和语音上下文学习基线，最高相对提升达46.8%。分析表明，对编码器（尤其是后层）进行导向比对语言模型主干更有效，说明导向机制通过调整高层声学与音素表征以更好地对齐预训练语言模型的表示空间，而非修改解码器。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 语音感知的大语言模型在域外设置下泛化能力差，现有方法依赖对比激活差异，效果有限，亟需一种更有效的轻量级适应策略。

Method: 提出SALSA方法，通过监督学习直接优化层间导向向量，实现对语音特征表示的精细化调节。

Result: 在多个跨域语音任务（如儿童语音、多语言、中英混用）上，SALSA显著优于零样本和上下文学习基线，性能提升最高达46.8%。

Conclusion: 对编码器（特别是后层）进行导向比对语言模型主干更有效，说明改进下游语音识别性能的关键在于对齐高层声学与音素表征与语言模型的表示空间，而非修改解码器。

Abstract: Speech-aware large language models often generalize poorly to out-of-domain settings. We propose SALSA (Speech-Aware LLM Adaptation via Learned Steering Activations), a lightweight adaptation method that learns layer-wise steering vectors. Unlike commonly used steering approaches that rely on contrastive activation differences, SALSA directly optimizes steering vectors using a supervised objective. Across children's speech, multilingual speech, and Mandarin-English code-switching benchmarks, SALSA substantially improves performance over zero-shot inference and speech in-context learning baselines, achieving up to 46.8% relative improvements over zero-shot. Analysis further demonstrates that steering the encoder, particularly the later layers, is more effective than steering the LLM backbone. These findings suggest that steering improves downstream ASR performance by adapting higher-level acoustic and phonetic representations to better align with the pretrained language model representation space, rather than by modifying the decoder itself.

</details>


### [76] [Short-form Text Rewriting with Phi Silica](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00462)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 小语言模型在短文本重写任务中面临语义保真度低和幻觉问题，而现有大模型虽表现良好但资源消耗大，亟需探索如何有效提升SLM在该场景下的性能。

Method: 采用数据集构建（从公开演示文稿中提取短篇展示文本）、提示蒸馏、参数高效微调，并利用GPT-5-chat生成重写标注及作为评判标准（LLM-as-a-judge）进行评估。

Conclusion: 通过对小语言模型进行数据、提示与参数层面的定向优化，可在短文本重写任务中显著缩小与大模型的差距，为实际应用中部署轻量级高精度重写系统提供了可行路径。

Abstract: Short-form text rewriting is a constrained variant of paraphrasing in which limited context and high semantic density leave little room for variation. While large language models perform well on general paraphrasing, small language models (SLMs) often struggle with semantic fidelity and hallucination robustness in short-form settings. In this work, we present an empirical study of adapting an SLM, Phi Silica, for short-form rewrite through dataset curation, prompt distillation, parameter-efficient fine-tuning, and evaluation. We curate a dataset of short presentation-style text from public slide decks and use GPT-5-chat both to generate rewrite supervision and to conduct LLM-as-a-judge evaluation. Our results show that finetuning improves semantic fidelity, reduces hallucinations, and increases preference win rate against GPT-5-chat rewrites. The findings suggest that targeted adaptation for SLMs can substantially narrow the gap to cloud models and provide practical guidance for adapting SLMs to precision-critical rewrite tasks.
