### [77] [On the Limits of LLM Adaptability: Impact of Model-Internalized Priors on Annotation Task Performance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00467)
*Etienne Casanova,Rafal Kocielnik,R. Michael Alvarez*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了大语言模型（LLMs）在零样本标注和LLM作为裁判任务中的可靠性，重点分析模型内部先验与用户指令之间的交互。通过跨多个数据集（社交媒体、游戏、新闻、论坛）的实验发现，近三分之二的零样本错误无法通过提示纠正，整体纠正率仅为34.8%；高置信度错误尤其难以修正。当任务定义存在偏差时，模型仍会遵循错误定义，且置信度保持不变。研究提出‘定义特定熟悉度’（DSF），发现其与模型性能呈正相关（偏相关系数r = +0.41），而文本级记忆指标（如ROUGE-L、BERTScore、嵌入余弦相似度）均未表现出正向关联。结论表明，提示修正存在局限性，任务定义对齐比文本记忆更重要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在零样本任务中广泛应用，但其可靠性受模型内部先验与用户指令之间交互的影响。现有方法依赖提示工程来纠正错误，但缺乏对错误可纠正性的系统评估，以及对模型如何理解任务定义的深入理解。因此需要揭示模型在不同条件下的行为模式，尤其是提示能否有效修正错误，以及任务定义对齐的重要性。

Method: 研究设计包括三个核心维度：(1) 模型对数据和任务定义的熟悉程度对性能的影响；(2) 提示中增加信息是否能纠正零样本错误（即“决策顽固性”）；(3) 模型对错误任务定义的敏感性。实验覆盖多种数据集（社交、游戏、新闻、论坛），使用密集模型与混合专家模型进行毒性检测任务。通过对比初始错误与提示后修正情况，计算纠正率，并引入定义特定熟悉度（DSF）衡量模型内部概念与任务定义的匹配程度。同时采用三种文本记忆指标（ROUGE-L、BERTScore、嵌入余弦相似度）进行对照分析。

Result: 近三分之二的零样本错误无法被提示纠正，整体纠正率仅为34.8%。高置信度错误尤为顽固。当任务定义存在偏差时，模型仍忠实执行但置信度不变。在控制数据集混杂因素后，定义特定熟悉度（DSF）与模型性能呈显著正相关（偏r = +0.41），而三种文本记忆指标均未表现出正向关联。

Conclusion: 提示修正在零样本标注任务中具有明显局限性，多数错误难以通过增加上下文信息纠正。模型表现更依赖于任务定义与模型内部认知的对齐程度，而非文本层面的记忆能力。因此，在构建LLM驱动的任务系统时，应优先确保任务定义清晰且与模型先验一致，而非依赖提示优化。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) are increasingly used for zero-shot annotation and LLM-as-a-judge tasks, yet their reliability hinges on how model-internalized priors interact with user-provided instructions. We investigate three dimensions of this interaction: (1) how an LLM's familiarity with data and task definitions affects performance, (2) the extent to which additional information in prompts can correct zero-shot errors ("decision stickiness"), and (3) model susceptibility to misaligned task definitions. Through experiments on toxicity detection across diverse datasets (spanning social media, gaming, news, and forums) using both dense and mixture-of-experts models, we find that nearly two-thirds of zero-shot errors are resistant to correction, with an overall rescue rate (fraction of initial errors corrected by prompting) of only 34.8%. High-confidence errors prove especially resistant to correction. When given misaligned definitions, LLMs follow them while maintaining confidence levels unchanged from the aligned condition. Crucially, we introduce Definition-Specific Familiarity (DSF), which measures alignment between a model's internal concept and the task definition. After controlling for dataset-level confounds, DSF shows a positive association with model performance (partial r = +0.41), while three distinct memorization metrics (ROUGE-L, BERTScore, and embedding cosine similarity) all fail to show a positive association. These findings show the limitations of prompt-based correction in annotation tasks, highlighting the importance of definition alignment over text-level memorization.

</details>


### [78] [Do Text Edits Generalize to Visual Generation? Benchmarking Cross-Modal Knowledge Editing in UMMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00477)
*Xin Gao,Cheng Yang,Chufan Shi,Taylor Berg-Kirkpatrick*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了UniKE，首个针对统一多模态模型（UMMs）跨模态知识编辑的基准测试，涵盖2,971个编辑主题。研究发现，尽管文本侧编辑效果可达92%，但直接图像生成下的VQA准确率仅18.5%，存在显著模态差距。为此提出基于推理增强的参数编辑方法，通过激活编辑后的知识提升图像生成性能，最多提升18.6个百分点。机制分析表明，文本表示与视觉生成条件路径之间对齐不充分是主要原因。研究指出，文本知识编辑不能保证可靠跨模态传递，呼吁发展模态感知的编辑方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着统一多模态模型在真实场景中广泛应用，如何有效更新其内部知识成为关键挑战。现有知识编辑技术虽在纯文本模型中成熟，但在多模态模型中是否能从文本编辑有效传递至图像生成仍不明确，亟需系统评估和改进方法。

Method: 提出UniKE基准，包含2,971个属性与关系编辑样本；采用基于VQA的视觉验证评估跨模态编辑效果；设计推理增强型参数编辑方法，显式激活编辑知识以指导图像生成。

Result: 文本侧编辑有效性达92%，但直接图像生成的最高VQA准确率为18.5%；所提方法使所有模型-编辑器组合的VQA准确率显著提升，最大提升达18.6个百分点；机制分析揭示文本表示与视觉生成路径间存在部分对齐问题。

Conclusion: 文本知识编辑无法确保可靠的跨模态转移，多模态模型中的知识编辑需考虑模态特性，应发展模态感知的编辑策略。

Abstract: Unified multimodal models (UMMs) have emerged as a promising paradigm for general-purpose multimodal intelligence. As they are deployed in real-world applications, effectively updating internal knowledge becomes critical. While knowledge editing has matured for text-only models, it remains unclear whether edits that successfully modify textual outputs also transfer to image generation in UMMs. To study this question, we introduce UniKE, the first benchmark for cross-modality knowledge editing in UMMs, comprising 2,971 edit subjects spanning attribute and relation edits. Using VQA-based visual verification, we reveal a striking modality gap: text-side efficacy can reach approximately 92%, whereas the best overall VQA accuracy under direct image generation is only 18.5%. We further propose Reasoning-augmented Parameter Editing, which explicitly activates edited knowledge before generation and improves overall VQA accuracy for all evaluated model-editor pairs, with gains up to 18.6 percentage points. Mechanistic analysis shows that this gap is associated with partial alignment between edited textual representations and the conditioning pathways for visual generation, where edits sufficient for text outputs may remain too weak or misaligned to steer image synthesis. These findings show that textual knowledge edits do not guarantee reliable cross-modality transfer and motivate modality-aware editing methods. Our code and data are available at https://github.com/gxx27/UniKE.

### [79] [LaSR: Context-Aware Speech Recognition via Latent Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00507)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Recent advances in Speech Large Language Models (Speech LLMs) have significantly enhanced spoken language understanding and reasoning. However, their contextual awareness is limited, struggling to perform speech recognition that effectively reflects the speaker's intent and topical context. In this paper, we propose LaSR (Latent Speech Reasoning), a novel training paradigm featuring a context-aware reasoning trajectory that leverages the latent reasoning process. Instead of generating explicit intermediate tokens, LaSR aligns chain-of-thought (CoT) supervision around the acoustic feature region of the targeted word, and introduces latent reasoning periods for context information grounding and transcriptional transition. Furthermore, to effectively benchmark contextual recognition on specialized vocabulary, we propose Spoken Darwin-Science, a large-scale corpus focusing on academic terminologies. Preliminary experiments on Fun-Audio-Chat demonstrate that LaSR significantly improves terminology recognition without introducing additional latency and consistently outperforms standard supervised fine-tuning baselines. Our findings highlight the potential of latent reasoning in building efficient, context-aware speech assistants.

### [80] [Skill or Skip? Learning Selective Skill Invocation in Agentic Tasks via Dual-Granularity Preference Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00510)
*Chishui Chen,Jiaye Lin,Te Sun,Junxi Wang,Yi Yang,Cong Qin,Yangen Hu,Lu Pan,Ke Zeng*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: SelSkill提出一种双粒度偏好学习框架，用于选择性地调用智能体技能。该方法将技能调用建模为‘调用或跳过’的决策问题，利用预测不确定性来优先选择候选决策点，并从共享轨迹前缀中构建受控的调用-跳过偏好对。同时结合回合级结果偏好与步骤级调用偏好，兼顾整体轨迹质量与技能调用的局部有效性。在ALFWorld、BFCL等任务上显著提升任务成功率和执行精度，且在零样本场景下表现出良好的跨领域泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法多关注技能选择或技能优化，但忽视了在当前决策点是否应调用相关技能的问题。不恰当的技能调用可能引入无关上下文，破坏正确的执行流程。

Method: 提出双粒度偏好学习框架SelSkill，将技能使用建模为调用或跳过决策；利用预测不确定性识别关键决策点；基于共享轨迹前缀构造可控的调用-跳过偏好对；融合回合级结果偏好与步骤级调用偏好以全面评估性能。

Result: 在ALFWorld（Qwen3-8B）上，任务成功率提升10.9个百分点，执行精度提升29.1个百分点；在BFCL上，任务成功率提升5.7个百分点，执行精度提升29.5个百分点；零样本测试在Tau-bench和PopQA上显示良好跨域泛化能力。

Conclusion: SelSkill通过精细化控制技能调用时机，有效提升了复杂任务中的执行准确性和成功率，并具备良好的零样本迁移能力，为智能体技能管理提供了新范式。

Abstract: Agent skills are callable procedural modules that provide reusable knowledge and execution policies for complex agentic tasks. However, existing methods mainly focus on selecting relevant skills or improving the skills themselves, while overlooking whether a relevant skill should actually be invoked at the current decision point. Unhelpful invocations may introduce irrelevant context and disrupt an otherwise correct execution process. To address this issue, we propose SelSkill, a dual-granularity preference-learning framework for selective skill invocation. SelSkill formulates skill use as a skill-or-skip decision, uses predictive uncertainty to prioritize candidate decision points, and constructs controlled invoke-skip preference pairs from shared trajectory prefixes. It further combines episode-level outcome preferences with step-level invocation preferences to capture both overall trajectory quality and the local effectiveness of skill invocation. On ALFWorld with Qwen3-8B, SelSkill improves task success by 10.9 percentage points and execution precision by 29.1 percentage points. On BFCL, it improves task success by 5.7 percentage points and execution precision by 29.5 percentage points. Zero-shot results on Tau-bench and PopQA further suggest that the learned invocation policy transfers to new domains with previously unseen skills.

</details>


### [81] [ProactiveLLM: Learning Active Interaction for Streaming Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00523)
*Junlong Tong,Yao Zhang,Anhao Zhao,Yingqi Fan,Yunpu Ma,Xiaoyu Shen*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: ProactiveLLM提出一种基于模型内生状态的主动交互机制，通过掩码流建模和同步特权自蒸馏（SPSD）训练方法，使模型在接收部分输入时即可感知语义充分性，从而动态决定何时进行交互。该方法无需外部标注或强教师信号，显著降低延迟并保持生成质量，适用于文本与语音流式任务。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准大语言模型采用读取后生成范式，导致延迟和计算开销；现有流式LLM虽能边接收边生成，但缺乏有效的交互时机判断机制，依赖硬编码或昂贵的外部对齐信号，因此需要一种无需外部监督的自适应交互决策方法。

Method: 提出ProactiveLLM，结合两种训练机制：1）基于单调随机掩码的流式建模，模拟逐步揭示的输入流，让模型学习从局部输入中捕捉语义依赖；2）同步特权自蒸馏（SPSD），将部分上下文的学生视图与同一模型生成的全上下文教师视图对齐，利用全信息指导不完整输入下的理解，从而诱导出内生的语义充分性提示。

Result: 在多个文本和语音流式任务上，ProactiveLLM显著降低了交互延迟，同时保持了高质量的输出，验证了其在动态、主动交互方面的有效性。

Conclusion: ProactiveLLM通过内生状态驱动交互决策，摆脱对外部标注或强教师的依赖，为流式LLM提供了可插拔、通用且高效的主动交互解决方案。

Abstract: Standard Large Language Models (LLMs) follow a read-then-generate paradigm, causing unnecessary latency and computation. Streaming LLMs alleviate this issue by generating while receiving inputs, but still struggle to decide when to interact with the stream. Existing methods either hard-code interaction timing or rely on costly external alignment signals, such as timing labels, reasoning trajectories, or stronger teachers. In this paper, we propose ProactiveLLM, which achieves active interaction by leveraging the model's endogenous states to guide interaction decisions. The model first learns to perceive semantic sufficiency from partial inputs through two complementary training mechanisms: mask-based streaming modeling and synchronized privileged self-distillation (SPSD). The former applies monotonic random masking to the input during training, simulating progressively revealed streaming inputs and enabling the model to learn local semantic dependencies from partial-input views. The latter aligns the partial-context student view with a full-context teacher view generated by the same evolving model, allowing privileged full-context evidence to guide the student's understanding under incomplete observations. Together, these mechanisms induce endogenous sufficiency cues without requiring external teachers or annotations, providing a versatile foundation for the plug-and-play integration of diverse decision heads. Extensive evaluation across text and speech streaming tasks confirms that ProactiveLLM significantly reduces interaction latency while maintaining quality, validating its capacity for dynamic and active interaction. Code is publicly available at https://github.com/EIT-NLP/StreamingLLM/tree/main/ProactiveLLM.

### [82] [Learning to Retrieve: Dual-Level Long-Term Memory for Text-to-SQL Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00547)
*Yibo Wang,Nikki Lijing Kuang,Philip S. Yu,Zhewei Yao,Yuxiong He*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: MERIT提出一种动态多时域记忆检索框架，通过episode-level（全局策略指导）和turn-level（局部决策支持）双层级记忆机制，结合强化学习优化检索策略。为解决中间阶段监督稀疏问题，引入轻量级过程奖励模型提供密集代理奖励。在BIRD-Interact和Spider2-Snow上均取得优于基线的性能，提升成功率并减少交互轮次，验证了多时域检索对经验复用的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有记忆检索方法在交互式文本到SQL任务中存在局限：静态方法依赖固定相似性规则，无法优化下游效用；动态方法仅基于最终结果学习，且在单一决策时域检索记忆，难以适应不同交互阶段的记忆需求变化。

Method: MERIT采用双层级记忆结构：episode-level记忆用于全局战略指导，turn-level记忆用于局部状态条件下的决策支持。两者均通过强化学习训练，其中turn-level检索利用轻量级过程奖励模型生成密集代理奖励以克服中间监督稀疏问题。

Result: 在BIRD-Interact上，MERIT显著提升成功率达到最优，同时减少平均交互轮次；在Spider2-Snow上的迁移实验表明其具备良好跨基准泛化能力，无需特定调优。

Conclusion: 多时域记忆检索能有效提升交互式文本到SQL代理中的经验复用能力，增强长期记忆在不同交互阶段的适应性与实用性。

Abstract: Interactive text-to-SQL agents solve database tasks through multi-turn interactions involving schema exploration, query execution, feedback interpretation, and decision revision. Long-term memory helps agents reuse past experiences, but existing retrieval methods remain limited. Static methods rely on fixed similarity heuristics that do not optimize downstream utility, while dynamic methods often learn from sparse final outcomes and retrieve memories at a single decision horizon. This is insufficient when memory usefulness changes across interaction stages, since memories useful for initial planning may differ from those needed for local, state-conditioned execution. We propose MERIT, a dynamic multi-horizon memory retrieval framework. MERIT maintains episode-level memory for global strategic guidance and turn-level memory for local decision support. Both levels use learned retrieval policies optimized with reinforcement learning. To train turn-level retrieval despite limited intermediate supervision, MERIT uses a lightweight Process Reward Model to provide dense proxy rewards for local memory selection. Experiments on BIRD-Interact show that MERIT outperforms no-memory, static-retrieval, and dynamic-retrieval baselines in success rate while reducing average interaction turns. Transfer results on Spider2-Snow further show positive cross-benchmark transfer without benchmark-specific tuning. These results suggest that multi-horizon retrieval improves experience reuse in interactive text-to-SQL agents.

### [83] [Revisiting Parameter-Based Knowledge Editing in Large Language Models: Theoretical Limits and Empirical Evidence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00570)
*Wanying Ren,Xin Song,Futing Wang,Guoxiu He,Aixin Sun*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文通过理论分析与实证评估，揭示了基于参数的知识编辑方法在实际应用中存在严重缺陷。研究提出‘维度坍缩假设’，解释局部权重修改会引发表示空间中脆弱方向的传播，导致全局干扰和推理崩溃。实验证明，现有参数编辑方法普遍损害大模型的核心能力，而简单的检索基线反而表现更优。结论强调未来研究应优先考虑知识编辑对模型基础能力的保护。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有参数化知识编辑方法忽视了其潜在的理论局限性，且缺乏在真实应用场景下的系统性评估，导致其有效性存疑。

Method: 提出维度坍缩假设，从理论上分析参数编辑的传播效应；设计多维度实验，系统考察知识复杂度、编辑数量、评估维度和基线方法的影响。

Result: 参数编辑方法普遍破坏大模型核心能力，而检索基线在所有条件下均优于参数编辑方法。

Abstract: Parameter-based knowledge editing updates the internal knowledge of large language models (LLMs) via localized weight modifications and has attracted significant attention. However, most existing methods overlook fundamental theoretical limitations and are rarely evaluated under realistic, practice-oriented settings. In this paper, we first present a theoretical analysis based on the dimensional Collapse Hypothesis, explaining how localized parameter edits can propagate along fragile directions in the representation space, inducing global interference and ultimately causing reasoning collapse. Building on this insight, we conduct a comprehensive empirical evaluation by systematically varying knowledge complexity, number of edits, evaluation dimensions, and baseline methods. Our results show that parameter-based editing methods consistently damage core LLM capabilities. In contrast, a simple retrieval-based baseline achieves consistently stronger performance than all parameter-editing methods across all evaluated conditions. These findings highlight that preserving the fundamental capabilities of LLMs after knowledge editing should be a central concern for future research.

### [84] [Sandboxed Coding Agents are Competitive Omni-modal Task Solvers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00579)

Method: 构建仅基于文本和图像输入的编码代理，利用沙盒化工具接口执行代码生成与工具调度，实现对音频视频内容中关键信息的提取；采用轨迹分析、失败分类、过程级追踪等方法评估性能与瓶颈；提出Code-X训练范式，结合轨迹数据集与可验证奖励机制进行技能增强；设计TerminalBench-O作为过程级多模态评测基准。

Result: 编码代理在多个音视频基准上表现媲美甚至优于主流原生多模态模型与预设多模态代理；技能注入显著提升性能；Code-X方案有效支持开放源码技能获取；TerminalBench-O为未来多模态处理提供了新的评测标准。

Conclusion: 多模态任务不一定需要原生多模态模型，通过代码驱动的工具调用与信息抽取策略，仅具文本+图像能力的代理同样可实现卓越性能。未来应聚焦于多模态处理能力的系统性提升，推动通用智能体向真实世界复杂任务演进。

Abstract: As multimodal LLMs increasingly target video and audio, it is often assumed that such tasks require native omnimodal models. We show that this is not always the case: coding agents with only text+image access and a sandboxed tool-use interface can match, and in several settings outperform, SOTA native omnimodal models and predefined multimodal agent scaffolds across multiple audio-video benchmarks. Our trajectory analysis suggests that their strength comes from writing code and orchestrating tools to extract relevant evidence from transcripts, frames, and other modality signals, thereby converting omnimodal tasks into retrieval and information-processing problems rather than ingesting entire media streams. We further characterize their limitations through a failure taxonomy and process-level trace analysis, and show that simple skill injection, including human-written and self-distilled skills, substantially improves performance. To explore open-source elicitation, we introduce Code-X, a training recipe with the OmniCoding trajectory dataset and verifiable reward, and provide baselines on Qwen-3.5-9B and Qwen-3.6-27B. Finally, we argue that the next frontier is many-modality processing, and introduce TerminalBench-O, a process-level benchmark for real-world omnimodal processing tasks. Code will be available at https://github.com/Dongping-Chen/OmniCoding.

### [85] [SPADER: Step-wise Peer Advantage with Diversity-Aware Exploration Rewards for Multi-Answer Question Answering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00593)
*Qiming Shi,Zhaolu Kang,Yunfan Zhou,Di Weng,Yingcai Wu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: SPADER 是一种用于多答案问答（Multi-Answer QA）的强化学习框架，针对长周期工具使用中的细粒度信用分配和探索奖励对齐问题。它引入了步骤级同伴优势（SPA）机制，通过并行轨迹间的比较进行无评判器的信用分配，并设计了多样性感知的探索奖励，以促进长尾实体发现。在 QAMPARI、Mintaka、WebQSP 和 QUEST 数据集上的实验表明，SPADER 在召回率和 F1 分数上优于基于提示的代理、结果监督的 RL 方法以及近期的步骤级监督方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 真实世界的问题往往需要发现多个有效答案，而非单一正确答案。现有方法大多聚焦于单答案任务，难以应对多答案问答中长期搜索轨迹中的信用分配难题以及对低频、长尾实体的探索激励不足的问题。

Method: 提出 SPADER 框架，包含两部分：(1) 步骤级同伴优势（SPA），一种无需评判器的逐步信用分配机制，通过比较并行轨迹的回报来估计优势；(2) 多样性感知探索奖励，通过加权稀有发现、降低冗余发现的奖励，鼓励模型探索更广泛的答案空间。

Result: 在 QAMPARI、Mintaka、WebQSP 与 QUEST 四个数据集上，SPADER 显著提升了召回率和整体 F1 分数，优于提示法代理、结果监督强化学习方法及当前先进的步骤级监督方法。

Conclusion: SPADER 为长周期多答案问答任务提供了一种有效的强化学习解决方案，通过精细的信用分配与探索激励机制，显著增强了模型发现多样且全面答案的能力。

Abstract: Large language models are increasingly deployed as tool-augmented agents to acquire information beyond parametric knowledge. While recent work has improved long-horizon tool-use reasoning, most approaches focus on tasks with a single correct answer. In contrast, many real-world queries require discovering a comprehensive set of valid answers, a setting known as Multi-Answer QA. This setting raises two challenges: fine-grained credit assignment over long search trajectories and reward alignment for sustained exploration beyond easy high-frequency entities. We propose SPADER, a reinforcement learning framework for long-horizon tool use in Multi-Answer QA. SPADER includes Step-wise Peer Advantage (SPA), a critic-free step-level credit assignment mechanism that aligns parallel trajectories by decision step and estimates advantages from peer returns. It also includes a diversity-aware exploration reward that promotes long-tail entity discovery by upweighting rare findings and downweighting redundant ones. Experiments on QAMPARI, Mintaka, WebQSP, and QUEST show that SPADER generally improves recall and overall F1 over prompting-based agents, outcome-supervised RL methods, and recent step-level supervision approaches. Our code and model weights are available at https://github.com/KhanCold/spader.

Yet existing evaluation paradigms remain anchored in task-based NLP benchmarks and fail to address interpretive validity, cultural situatedness, and epistemic mediation. This paper reconceptualizes multilingual reasoning LLMs as hermeneutic instruments that actively structure meaning production across linguistic and cultural contexts. ### [87] [Linguistics-Aware Non-Distortionary LLM Watermarking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00613)
*Shinwoo Park,Hyejin Park,Hyeseon An,Yo-Sub Han*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: LUNA is a linguistically adaptive watermarking method for multilingual language models that enables model-free detection and maintains text quality through non-distortionary sampling. It uses part-of-speech context from external corpora to estimate entropy and control a binary tournament sampler, allowing the detector to reconstruct watermark schedules using only public tools and a secret key. Evaluated across six diverse languages and two domains, LUNA achieves superior performance with an AUROC of 0.9959, minimal perplexity shift (0.045), and strong consistency in text quality metrics.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Existing watermarking methods struggle in multilingual settings due to variations in morphology, segmentation, and scripts, which affect where watermark signals can be naturally embedded. Current approaches often degrade text quality or require trust in the model provider for verification. LUNA addresses these challenges by enabling robust, model-free detection while preserving output quality across diverse linguistic environments.

Method: LUNA combines model-free detection with single-token non-distortion under the random-key watermarking framework. It estimates normalized next-tag entropy based on part-of-speech contexts from an external corpus, then uses this to set the depth of a non-distortionary binary tournament sampler. The detector reconstructs the watermark schedule using the same public components: text, tokenizer, tagger, and secret key.

Result: LUNA achieves an AUROC of 0.9959 and a mean absolute median perplexity shift of 0.045 across 12 evaluation settings—lower than all eight baselines. Its 95% bootstrap interval [0.022, 0.073] falls entirely below baseline intervals. It also shows the lowest shifts in Self-BLEU, Distinct-1, surprisal, and entropy. Crucially, LUNA is the only method achieving AUROC > 0.99 and perplexity shift < 0.1 in 9 out of 12 settings, while no baseline exceeds 2 such cases.

Conclusion: LUNA provides a highly effective, linguistically adaptive watermarking solution for multilingual language models. By leveraging POS-based entropy estimation and non-distortionary sampling, it ensures high detection accuracy without degrading text quality, even in diverse linguistic and domain contexts. Its model-free detection and open implementation make it practical and trustworthy for real-world deployment.

Abstract: Watermarking should identify language-model output without degrading quality or limiting verification to the model provider. Multilingual deployment makes this harder because morphology, segmentation, and script change where watermark evidence can enter naturally. We introduce LUNA, a linguistically adaptive watermark that combines model-free detection with single-token non-distortion under the standard random-key model. LUNA estimates normalized next-tag entropy from part-of-speech contexts in an external corpus and uses it to set the depth of a non-distortionary binary tournament sampler; the detector reconstructs the same schedule from text, a tokenizer, a tagger, and a secret key. We evaluate six typologically diverse languages and two domains against eight primary baselines. LUNA attains an AUROC of 0.9959 and the lowest mean absolute median perplexity shift of 0.045 across the twelve settings; its 95% bootstrap interval [0.022, 0.073] lies below all baseline intervals. LUNA also records the lowest mean Self-BLEU, Distinct-1, surprisal, and entropy shifts. It is the only method that simultaneously achieves AUROC > 0.99 and an absolute median perplexity shift below 0.1 in a majority of settings, reaching this regime in 9 of the 12 settings while no baseline reaches it in more than 2. Our code is available at: https://github.com/Shinwoo-Park/luna_watermark

### [88] [MemPro: Agentic Memory Systems as Evolvable Programs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00619)
*Qingshan Liu,Guoqing Wang,Wen Wu,Jingqi Huang,Xinqi Tao,Dejia Song,Jie Zhou,Liang He*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: MemPro 是一个系统级演进框架，将记忆构建-检索（MCR）管道视为可演化的程序，而非仅调整记忆库或提示文本。通过维护可运行的记忆系统实现版本树，进化代理迭代选择优秀版本，诊断失败模式，并通过故障导向的编辑-调试-优化生成改进版本。在 LongMemEval、LoCoMo、HotpotQA 和 NarrativeQA 上的实验表明，MemPro 在少数迭代内优于静态和提示级演化基线，且持续改进，具备良好的性能-成本权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有代理记忆系统通常只在部署后调整记忆库，而保持整个管道固定，难以应对异构的任务特定失败模式，且与随时间演变的记忆库结构不匹配。

Method: MemPro 采用版本树维护可运行的记忆系统实现，通过进化代理选择候选版本，诊断失败模式，并基于故障模式进行编辑-调试-优化以生成更优子版本。

Result: 在 LongMemEval、LoCoMo、HotpotQA 和 NarrativeQA 上，MemPro 在少量迭代内即超越强基线，性能持续提升，且在性能与成本之间取得良好平衡。

Conclusion: MemPro 通过将整个 MCR 管道视为可演化程序，有效解决了传统方法中因固定管道导致的适应性差问题，实现了高效、持续的系统演化。

Abstract: Long-horizon autonomous agents require memory systems to retain historical information, track evolving states, and reuse relevant knowledge beyond finite context windows. Existing agentic memory systems typically follow a memory construction-retrieval (MCR) pipeline, but often adapt mainly the memory bank while keeping the surrounding pipeline fixed after deployment. This fixed-pipeline design struggles to handle heterogeneous task-specific failure modes and can become misaligned with memory banks that evolve in scale and structure over time. To address these limitations, we propose MemPro, a system-level evolution framework that treats the entire MCR pipeline as an evolvable program rather than adapting only the memory bank or prompt text. MemPro maintains a version tree of runnable memory-system implementations, where an Evolving Agent iteratively selects promising versions, diagnoses recurring failures, and creates improved child versions through failure-mode-guided edit-debug refinement. Experiments on LongMemEval, LoCoMo, HotpotQA, and NarrativeQA show that MemPro consistently outperforms strong static and prompt-level evolving baselines within a few iterations, continues to improve with evolution, and achieves a favorable performance-cost trade-off. Code is available at https://github.com/wanghai673/MemPro.

</details>


### [89] [Robust Reasoning via Dynamic Token Selection for Distribution-Aligned Self-Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00628)
*Ruiqi Zhang,Lingxiang Wang,Hainan Zhang Zhiming Zheng*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为分布对齐自蒸馏（DASD）的新方法，旨在解决自蒸馏过程中因模仿参考答案风格而导致的表面形式偏差问题。通过使用答案感知的参考模型生成候选词元，并根据基础模型的置信度动态过滤，DASD能够保留有益的逻辑知识，同时抑制分布不一致的风格噪声。实验表明，DASD在数学、代码和常识推理任务上均优于现有基线，减少高困惑度词元数量，并提升不同难度任务下的鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自蒸馏虽能提高学习效率，但参考答案引入的强烈风格偏差使生成模型倾向于模仿表面形式而非学习有效的推理模式，尤其在高困惑度词元存在时可能破坏模型原始分布，影响复杂推理任务的表现。

Method: 提出分布对齐自蒸馏（DASD），利用答案感知的参考模型生成候选词元，并基于基础模型的置信度动态筛选，以保留逻辑知识并抑制风格噪声。

Result: DASD在数学、代码和常识推理基准测试中持续优于竞争基线，显著降低高困惑度词元比例，增强模型在各类难度任务上的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: DASD通过智能过滤高困惑度词元，有效平衡了知识保留与风格控制，在不破坏模型原始分布的前提下提升了推理能力与泛化性能。

Abstract: Self-distillation improves learning efficiency by rewriting reference answers as training data that better matches the model's own distribution. However, reference answers also introduce strong stylistic biases, causing the generative model to imitate surface forms rather than learn useful reasoning patterns. We observe that the rewriting data contains a large number of high-perplexity (PPL) tokens, coming from two distinct sources: beneficial knowledge-enhancing logical corrections, and harmful stylistic drift induced by reference imitation. Treating all such tokens equally can disrupt the base model's original distribution and degrade performance, especially on difficult reasoning tasks. To address this, we propose Distribution-Aligned Self-Distillation (DASD), which uses an answer-aware reference model to generate candidate tokens and dynamically filters them according to the base model's confidence. DASD preserves tokens that encode useful logical knowledge while suppressing distributionally misaligned style noise. Experiments on math, code, and commonsense reasoning benchmarks show that DASD consistently outperforms competitive baselines, reduces high-PPL tokens, and improves robustness across tasks of varying difficulty.

### [91] [BitsMoE: Efficient Spectral Energy-Guided Bit Allocation for MoE LLM Quantization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00079)
*Jiayu Zhao,Zihan Teng,Minhao Fan,Tianrui Ma,Wentao Ren,Song Chen,Weichen Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: BitsMoE提出了一种基于谱-能量引导的比特分配框架，用于Mixture-of-Experts（MoE）大语言模型的量化。该方法通过奇异值分解（SVD）将每个MoE层分解为共享基底和专家特定的谱因子，保留共享基底不进行量化以维持跨专家的通用结构，并利用专家特定因子作为细粒度量化单元。为了确定每个单元的比特宽度，BitsMoE将谱级混合精度量化建模为激活感知的重构代理，并求解一个在固定比特预算下最小化估计重构损失的整数线性规划问题。实验表明，在多个MoE LLM上，BitsMoE显著降低了超低比特场景下的下游任务准确率下降。在Qwen3-30B-A3B-Base上进行2比特量化时，相比GPTQ，BitsMoE加速量化12.3倍，平均准确率提升27.83个百分点，解码速度提高1.76倍。模型与代码已公开于GitHub。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有MoE压缩方法在超低比特量化下表现不佳：剪枝会不可逆地损失模型容量，而粗粒度量化无法根据专家和权重方向的重要性合理分配比特。因此需要一种能精细控制比特分配、同时保留关键结构信息的量化方法。

Method: 提出基于谱-能量引导的比特分配框架BitsMoE，通过SVD分解MoE层为共享基底与专家特定谱因子，保留共享基底不变，对专家特定因子进行细粒度量化；设计激活感知的重构损失函数，并求解整数线性规划以在固定比特预算下最小化重构误差。

Result: 在多个MoE LLM上验证，2比特量化下相较GPTQ，BitsMoE实现12.3倍量化加速、27.83%平均准确率提升、1.76倍解码速度提升，显著优于现有方法。

Conclusion: BitsMoE有效解决了MoE模型在超低比特量化中的内存与性能瓶颈，通过谱分解与智能比特分配，在保持高精度的同时大幅降低计算开销，具备实用价值与推广潜力。

Abstract: Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) large language models reduce per-token computation through sparse expert activation, but their deployment remains memory-intensive because all expert weights must be kept resident in memory. Existing MoE compression methods struggle in the ultra-low-bit regime: pruning irreversibly removes model capacity, while coarse-grained quantization fails to allocate bits according to heterogeneous expert and weight-direction importance. We propose BitsMoE, a spectral-energy-guided bit-allocation framework for MoE LLM quantization. BitsMoE decomposes each MoE layer by SVD into a shared basis and expert-specific spectral factors, retaining the shared basis without quantization to preserve common cross-expert structure and using the expert-specific factors as fine-grained quantization units. To determine the bit-width of each unit, BitsMoE formulates spectrum-wise mixed-precision quantization as an activation-aware reconstruction surrogate and solves an integer linear program that minimizes estimated reconstruction loss under a fixed bit budget. Experiments across multiple MoE LLMs show that BitsMoE substantially reduces downstream task accuracy degradation in ultra-low-bit regimes. Under 2-bit quantization on Qwen3-30B-A3B-Base, BitsMoE accelerates quantization by 12.3$\times$, improves average accuracy by 27.83 percentage points, and increases decoding speed by 1.76$\times$ over GPTQ. Our model and code are publicly available at https://github.com/zjiayu064/BitsMoE.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有深度学习方法在处理高维、复杂时空模式的分布式声学传感（DAS）数据时，难以有效捕捉长距离依赖关系，且处理原始信号计算成本过高。

Method: 采用基于ANOVA选择的24个时域、波形域和频域统计特征作为输入，构建多分支Transformer结构，每个域通过专用的逐步注意力和通道注意力分支处理，最终通过自适应门控机制融合。

Abstract: Distributed Acoustic Sensing (DAS) enables large-scale monitoring through optical fibers, but its high dimensionality and complex spatio-temporal patterns make event classification demanding. Existing deep learning approaches-CNNs, recurrent models, and Transformer variants-either fail to capture long-range dependencies or require processing raw DAS matrices at prohibitive cost. We propose DAStatFormer, a hybrid multibranch Transformer that combines compact multidomain statistical features with Gated Transformer Networks. Instead of raw signals, we extract 24 ANOVA-selected attributes per channel from the temporal, waveform, and spectral domains, reducing data size by orders of magnitude while preserving discriminative information. Each domain is processed via dedicated step-wise and channel-wise attention branches, fused by an adaptive gating mechanism. Experiments on the open $Φ$-OTDR benchmark and a real-scenario DAS dataset show that DAS-tatFormer achieves up to 99.4% accuracy and near-perfect real-world performance, while using significantly fewer parameters and lower inference cost than models such as DASFormer and DeepViT. These results demonstrate its suitability for scalable, real-time DAS-based monitoring. We release our code at https://github.com/MichelD-git/DAStatFormer

### [93] [Hoeffding Concept Bottleneck Models with Applications to Overhead Images](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00082)
*Clément Bénard,Manon Arfib,Christophe Labreuche,Victor Quétu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出Hoeffding概念瓶颈模型（HCBM），通过非线性、稀疏的概念得分聚合方式，提升深度学习在计算机视觉任务中的可解释性。相较于传统线性概念聚合方法，HCBM利用梯度提升树的Hoeffding分解和主要析取项生成紧凑预测，有效缓解概念间信息泄漏问题，并在分类与目标检测任务中表现更优。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有概念瓶颈模型（CBM）依赖线性聚合概念得分，导致概念数量多、可解释性下降及信息泄露问题；且概念与输出之间的关系通常非线性，因此需要更优的建模方式以增强可解释性与性能。

Method: 基于Hoeffding功能分解构建非线性、稀疏的概念聚合机制，利用梯度提升树框架提取关键概念组合（即主要析取项），实现紧凑且可解释的预测输出。

Result: HCBM在多个分类和目标检测任务中均优于传统线性CBM，具备更强的鲁棒性和更低的信息泄漏风险，尤其在航拍图像等复杂场景下表现突出。

Abstract: Explainability of deep learning algorithms is critical for computer-vision applications with high-stake decisions. Concept bottleneck models (CBM) have recently shown promising performance to provide explainable and accurate predictions for classification problems, based on a bottleneck of high-level concepts. Existing CBM methods rely on a linear aggregation of the concept scores to compute predictions. However, a large number of concepts is often used in this linear approach, which undermines explainability and favors information leakage. In general, the underlying relation between concepts and output logits is not linear. Therefore, we introduce Hoeffding Concept Bottleneck Models (HCBM), which build on the Hoeffding functional decomposition of gradient-boosted trees to provide non-linear and sparse aggregations of concept scores, and generate compact predictions using prime implicants. HCBM are proved to be robust to interconcept leakage, and outperform standard linear CBM in practice, as shown in extensive experiments. Beyond classification, HCBM can be adapted to object detection, and we focus on a challenging case with overhead images to show the high performance of HCBM in these settings.

### [94] [From Demonstrations to Rewards: Test-Time Prompt Optimization for VLM Reward Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00083)
*Christian Gumbsch,Leonardo Barcellona,Lennard Schünemann,Platon Karageorgis,Andrii Zadaianchuk,Zehao Wang,Sergey Zakharov,Fabien Despinoy,Rahaf Aljundi,Efstratios Gavves*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过少量专家示范数据，在测试阶段对预训练视觉-语言模型的奖励模型进行语言指令优化，采用提示工程方式减少假阳性预测，同时保持真阳性，不依赖额外模型训练或计算开销。

Conclusion: Demo2Reward是一种高效、轻量且可泛化的测试时适应方法，有效利用少量示范数据优化奖励模型，为无监督或弱监督机器人学习提供了实用解决方案。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning relies on accurate reward functions, which are often hand-crafted or even unavailable in real-world applications, such as robotics. Recent work has explored the zero-shot reasoning capabilities of pre-trained Vision-Language Models (VLMs) as reward models. However, without careful prompt engineering, these approaches tend to produce suboptimal rewards, where false positive predictions can severely degrade downstream policy learning. In robotics, limited datasets comprising expert demonstrations are often collected to bootstrap policy learning. This scenario provides an opportunity to optimize a reward model prior policy training. We propose Demo2Reward a test-time adaptation technique to optimize the language instruction of a reward model based on a few demonstrations (3-10 trajectories) to reduce false positives while preserving true positives. Crucially, this requires no additional model training or computation resources during policy learning. We show that Demo2Reward consistently outperforms existing zero- and few-shot VLM reward models across a range of simulated robotic tasks and policy backbones. Finally, we demonstrate that Demo2Reward effectively transfers to a real-world robotic learning scenario, enabling policy learning without manually engineering a reward function.

### [95] [A Shared Valence Axis Across Modern LLMs and Human EEG: The Saturation Regularity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00129)
*Yousef A. Radwan,Xuhui Liu,Kilichbek Haydarov,Yuqian Fu,Mohamed Elhoseiny*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究探索现代大语言模型（LLM）是否可作为理解人类大脑神经表征的工具，聚焦于脑电图（EEG）中的情感效价。研究构建了一个仅基于九个情绪诱发句子的一维效价轴（V-axis），并通过零样本迁移和跨模型一致性验证其有效性。结果发现，该轴能有效映射到人类神经活动：在123名受试者观看情感视频的公开EEG数据集中，单一线性投影即可追踪每个刺激的V轴位置；此外，36个未接触V轴的EEG情绪分类器在内部表示中自发重现了相同效价结构，表明语言模型与人类电生理活动存在共同的效价表征。然而，这种收敛并未提供有效的训练信号——测试25种对齐策略后发现，多数方法反而降低解码性能，16种显著损害准确率。研究提出“饱和正则性”：当任务标签已将脑解码网络引导至目标方向后，额外监督主要扭曲已饱和的基域，而承载类内差异的残差子空间几乎得不到有用梯度。据此，研究转而通过集成残差多样性而非强化基域监督，在FACED数据集上提升平衡准确率10.5%，该效果也在SEED-V数据集中复现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究大语言模型能否作为理解人类大脑神经表征的工具，特别是情感效价在脑电图中的表现，以揭示语言模型与人类认知之间的潜在关联。

Method: 构建基于九个情绪诱发句子的一维效价轴（V-axis），通过零样本迁移与跨模型一致性验证；在公开EEG数据集上进行线性投影分析，并训练36个未接触V轴的情绪分类器观察其内部表示；测试25种对齐策略评估其对解码性能的影响；提出‘饱和正则性’理论，并采用残差多样性集成策略优化性能。

Result: LLM衍生的效价轴能有效映射人类神经活动，且多个独立训练的分类器自发重现该结构；但大多数对齐策略损害性能，仅通过集成残差多样性实现显著性能提升（FACED上+10.5%平衡准确率，SEED-V上复现）。

Conclusion: 大语言模型可作为理解人类情感效价神经表征的有效工具，但传统监督对齐会因饱和而失效。真正的改进应来自对残差子空间的利用，通过多样性集成实现性能突破。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have emerged as powerful representation learners whose internal features increasingly align with human cognition. We study whether modern LLMs can serve as a lens for understanding neural representations in the human brain, focusing on emotional valence in EEG.
  We first build a one-dimensional valence direction, the V-axis, from modern LLMs using only nine emotion-evocative sentences. We validate it through zero-shot transfer to sentiment benchmarks and cross-model consistency across fourteen LLMs. We then show that this LLM-derived direction maps onto human neural activity. On a public EEG cohort of 123 subjects watching affective videos, a single linear projection on EEG features tracks the V-axis position of each stimulus. Moreover, 36 EEG emotion classifiers trained without exposure to the V-axis spontaneously rediscover the same direction in their internal representations, suggesting that the same valence structure emerges in both language models and human electrophysiology.
  Yet this convergence does not provide an effective training signal. We test twenty-five alignment strategies, including knowledge distillation, representational similarity, contrastive, and topographic losses; none improve decoding, and sixteen significantly reduce accuracy. We formalize this result as the saturation regularity: once task labels alone drive a brain-decoding network onto the target direction, additional supervision mainly distorts an already-saturated basin, while the load-bearing within-class residual receives little useful gradient.
  This regularity also indicates where improvement should come from: the residual subspace unreachable by supervision. Motivated by this insight, we ensemble across residual diversity rather than supervising the basin, improving balanced accuracy by 10.5% over the prior best on FACED, with the same effect replicated on SEED-V.

</details>


### [96] [Automatically Differentiable Nonlinear Tensor Networks (ADNTNs) for Exponential Compression of Deep Neural Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00130)
*Andrzej Cichocki,Michal Wietczak*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种名为自动微分非线性张量网络（ADNTN）的结构化权重生成器，通过反向自动微分端到端训练紧凑的核心张量。ADNTN扩展了低秩适应和张量分解方法，利用小核心、非线性激活和可选的横向混合张量构建大型权重张量，包含三种架构：树形张量网络（TTN）、带边界解纠缠器的增强型TTN（aTTN）以及多尺度纠缠重整化组态（MERA）。该方法支持非线性激活、任务感知目标、批处理和硬件感知执行调度，但不消除大中间结果、不良收缩顺序或一般环状张量网络精确收缩的成本。在AlexNet和VGG-16层上的大量模拟显示，每层压缩比可达2000×至77000×，准确率通常与密集基线相当，甚至在某些VGG-16情况下有所提升。这些结果表明ADNTN是一种有前景的、数学结构清晰且硬件友好的小型神经网络路径，前提是优化、收缩调度和部署内核需协同设计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有神经网络压缩方法在保持模型性能的同时难以实现极高的压缩比，尤其在深层网络中面临结构复杂性和计算效率的挑战。为解决这一问题，本文提出一种结合自动微分与张量网络结构的新方法，旨在通过更紧凑的参数化方式实现高效、可扩展的模型压缩，同时保持对硬件特性的敏感性。

Method: 采用反向模式自动微分对紧凑核心张量进行端到端训练；利用层次化的小型核心张量、非线性激活函数及可选的横向混合张量构建大型权重张量；设计了三种具体架构（TTN、aTTN、MERA），支持任务感知目标、批量处理和硬件感知执行调度；通过优化收缩顺序与部署内核实现高效计算。

Result: 在AlexNet和VGG-16模型的多个层上实现了2000×至77000×的压缩比，多数情况下精度接近或优于原始密集模型，部分场景下显著提升，验证了方法的有效性与潜力。

Conclusion: ADNTN提供了一种数学结构清晰、硬件感知强且极具压缩潜力的神经网络轻量化路径，未来工作应聚焦于联合优化算法、收缩策略与部署实现，以进一步释放其性能上限。

Abstract: We study Automatically Differentiable Nonlinear Tensor Networks (ADNTNs), a family of structured weight generators whose compact core tensors are trained end-to-end by reverse-mode automatic differentiation (AD). The approach can be viewed as a natural extension of low-rank adaptation and tensor factorisation: instead of using one low-rank matrix update, an ADNTN builds a large weight tensor through a hierarchy of small cores, nonlinear activations, and optional lateral mixing tensors. The paper focuses on three architectures: Tree Tensor Networks (TTNs), augmented TTNs (aTTNs) with boundary disentanglers, and Multi-scale Entanglement Renormalisation Ansatze (MERA).
  The formulation supports nonlinear activations, task-aware objectives, batching, and hardware-aware execution schedules. At the same time, the paper keeps a clear distinction between \emph{differentiating} a contraction program and making contraction free: AD does not remove the cost of large intermediates, poor contraction orders, or exact contraction of general loopy tensor networks.
  Extensive simulations on AlexNet and VGG-16 layers show per-layer compression ratios from roughly $2000\times$ to $77000\times$ in the studied settings, with accuracy often matching the dense baseline and, in several VGG-16 cases, improving it. These results are encouraging rather than final: they suggest that ADNTNs are a promising, mathematically structured, and hardware-aware route toward much smaller neural networks, provided that optimisation, contraction schedules, and deployment kernels are designed together.

</details>


### [97] [Foundation-Preserving Adaptation via Generalized Rayleigh-Quotient Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00132)
*Dongjun Kim,Adrian de Wynter,Huancheng Chen,Heasung Kim,Haris Vikalo*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: FoLoRA 是一种遗忘感知的优化框架，通过引入基于一阶保持条件的遗忘惩罚和任务效用，利用广义瑞利商对更新方向进行评分，实现任务效用与遗忘惩罚的平衡。它采用谱坐标系统指导门控Adam更新，抑制低效用高遗忘的方向，并通过采样预训练模型构建预训练代理校准数据，避免依赖单一代理数据集。在数学、代码和指令遵循等任务上的实验表明，FoLoRA 在保持非目标能力方面优于基线方法，同时提升目标任务性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有微调方法在适应下游任务时容易损害预训练阶段获得的非目标能力，而现有遗忘感知方法多依赖固定初始化或约束，无法动态调节适应与保持之间的权衡。因此需要一种能有效平衡任务适应性与预训练知识保留的新方法。

Method: FoLoRA 提出基于一阶保持条件的遗忘惩罚，结合预训练代理激活与下游任务激活定义任务效用。通过广义瑞利商计算任务效用与遗忘惩罚之比，构建谱坐标系统，实现方向性门控Adam更新，动态抑制低效用高遗忘方向。同时，通过从预训练模型中采样生成预训练代理校准数据，提升遗忘评估的鲁棒性。

Result: 在数学、代码生成和指令遵循等任务上，FoLoRA 显著提升了目标任务性能，并在非目标能力的综合保留上优于所有基线方法，表现出更强的适应与保持平衡能力。

Conclusion: FoLoRA 通过动态调节更新方向，在微调过程中有效平衡了任务适应性与预训练知识保留，是一种高效的遗忘感知优化框架，适用于多种下游任务。

Abstract: While finetuning effectively adapts foundation models to specialized downstream tasks, it can degrade nontarget capabilities acquired during pretraining. Existing forgetting aware methods typically seek safer updates through specialized initialization or fixed constraints, but do not regulate the adaptation preservation trade-off during training. We propose Foundation Preserving LoRA (FoLoRA), a forgetting aware optimization framework. Guided by a first order preservation condition, FoLoRA defines a forgetting penalty over pretraining-proxy activations and a task utility over downstream task activations. It then scores update directions by task utility per unit forgetting penalty via a generalized Rayleigh quotient. The resulting spectral coordinate system enables direction wise gated Adam updates, attenuating low utility to penalty directions during training. To estimate the forgetting penalty, FoLoRA constructs pretraining proxy calibration data by sampling from the pretrained model rather than relying on a single proxy dataset. Experiments on math, code, and instruction following adaptation show that FoLoRA achieves the strongest preservation adaptation balance over baselines, improving target task performance with best aggregate preservation of non target capabilities.

</details>

Method: 构建四维多轴分类体系：(i) 架构维度（表示形式、动态建模、输入模态、学习范式、下游应用）；(ii) 方法族（状态空间与递归模型、Transformer、扩散模型、物理信息网络、语言增强多模态系统）；(iii) 推理策略（基于想象的规划、潜在策略学习、反事实推理、不确定性下的规划）；(iv) 应用领域（机器人、自动驾驶、视频预测、多模态智能体、强化学习、科学建模、医学影像、教育测量、金融等），并结合代表性系统进行分析与评估。

Result: 揭示了世界模型各维度间的交互关系，识别出当前关键挑战如预测误差累积、仿真到现实迁移困难、评估标准不统一等问题，并提出迈向统一多模态世界模型、大规模交互式模拟器及安全应用的未来路径。

Conclusion: 世界模型正朝着更统一、更强大、更安全的方向发展，融合思维链推理与环境想象能力，未来有望在复杂任务中实现通用智能的突破。

Abstract: World models, internal simulators that learn the structure and dynamics of an environment, have emerged as a central paradigm in the pursuit of artificial general intelligence, enabling agents to predict, plan, and reason within learned representations. Despite rapid progress across reinforcement learning, robotics, autonomous driving, and video generation, the field lacks a unified framework integrating its diverse architectural choices, training methods, reasoning mechanisms, and application settings. This survey addresses that gap with a multi-axis taxonomy organized along four dimensions: (i) architecture, encompassing representation format, dynamics formulation, input modality, learning paradigm, and downstream application; (ii) methodological family, including state-space and recurrent approaches, transformer-based models, diffusion-based generators, physics-informed networks, and language-augmented multimodal systems; (iii) reasoning strategy, covering imagination-based planning, latent policy learning, counterfactual reasoning, and planning under uncertainty; and (iv) application domain, spanning robotics, autonomous driving, video prediction, multimodal agents, reinforcement learning, scientific modeling, medical imaging, educational measurement, and business and finance. Tracing the field from early cognitive-science foundations to milestone systems such as PlaNet, the Dreamer family, MuZero, Sora, Cosmos, and Genie, we examine how these dimensions interact and highlight the recent convergence of chain-of-thought reasoning with world-model imagination. We review evaluation protocols and benchmarks, identify persistent challenges such as compounding prediction errors, sim-to-real transfer, and fragmented evaluation, and outline future directions toward unified multimodal world models, foundation-scale interactive simulators, and safe deployment in safety-critical domains.

### [99] [On Effectiveness and Efficiency of Agentic Tool-calling and RL Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00135)
*Tong Liu,Cheng Qian,Matej Cief,Yuan He,Daniele Dan,Nikolaos Aletras,Gabriella Kazai*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究大语言模型代理中的工具调用能力，从有效性和效率两个维度展开。在有效性方面，系统分析了工具调用评估流程，发现结果对随机种子、系统提示、多轮模板构建及历史信息传递等细微实现细节高度敏感，导致排行榜在多轮场景下不可靠。在效率方面，识别出强化学习训练中的两大计算浪费：（i）大量提示无学习信号，（ii）策略更新计算成本高。基于此，提出两项加速技术，在不降低性能的前提下显著提升训练速度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有工具调用评估缺乏标准化，导致性能结果不可靠；同时，强化学习训练过程存在大量计算浪费，影响训练效率。

Method: 系统分析工具调用评估流程中各实现细节的影响；识别强化学习训练中的计算浪费来源；设计并验证两项加速技术以提升训练效率。

Result: 揭示了评估实现细节对性能结果的显著影响，证明了多轮设置下排行榜的不可靠性；提出的加速技术实现了显著的墙钟时间提速，且未损害模型性能。

Conclusion: 工具调用的评估需建立严格标准化流程，否则结果不可信；通过优化强化学习训练过程，可大幅提高效率，为高效训练工具调用模型提供可行路径。

Abstract: Tool-calling is a central component of modern large language model (LLM) agents, equipping them with skills beyond their parametric knowledge. This paper studies tool-calling along two complementary axes: effectiveness, i.e., how this capability is measured, and efficiency, i.e., how it is learned. On effectiveness, we systematically analyze tool-calling evaluation pipelines and show that results can be highly sensitive to seemingly minor, often undocumented implementation choices including the random seed, system prompt, multi-turn template construction, and how prior interaction/reasoning history is carried forward. These choices can lead to substantial differences in reported performance, especially in multi-turn settings where without rigorous standardization, leaderboard rankings are unreliable. On efficiency, we examine standard reinforcement learning (RL) for tool-calling and identify two sources of computational waste: (i) during rollouts, many prompts produce no learning signal, and (ii) during policy updates, optimization incurs high computational cost. Guided by these findings, we introduce two techniques that accelerate RL-based tool-calling training, achieving substantial wall-clock speedup without degrading performance.

Abstract: The proliferation of adversarial synthetic content, accelerated by Generative AI (GenAI) is rendering traditional reactive detection methods ineffective. This survey synthesizes emerging research to demonstrate a paradigm shift toward the proactive detection of emerging inauthentic narratives. By structuring the analysis around the C5 Interaction Model (Context, Causes, Content, Cycle of Amplification, Consequences), we integrate different research streams from machine learning and social science. To differentiate spread patterns of synthetic amplification from authentic baseline traffic, this paper surveys state-of-the-art techniques for modeling the creation, seeding, and propagation of fresh narratives, including the analysis of Coordinated Inauthentic Behavior (CIB), epidemiological modeling, and Hawkes process. This survey also provides a systematic review of proactive detection methods for adversarial threats at different stages in the C5 interaction model, specifically, anomaly detection in high-dimensional embedding spaces, unsupervised coordination detection on multi-layer graphs, and agentic AI systems. Finally, this survey addresses challenges posed by GenAI, including the difficulty of tracking rapidly changing threats and multi-level distributional drift, and it outlines a future research agenda focused on detecting anomalous clusters and building anticipatory and resilient systems. This survey provides a comprehensive, lifecycle-based review of methods for the proactive detection of emerging synthetic threats for more resilient information ecosystems.

In this work, we introduce GEM, a simple but highly effective erasure framework for Rectified Flow models. As part of our contribution, we establish a principled bridge between trajectory-based unlearning grounded in Generative Flow Networks and classic teacher-guided erasure: we translate trajectory-based signals into a teacher-guided flow-matching setup that unifies the strengths of both paradigms. ### [102] [Adaptive data selection improves wearable prediction under low baseline performance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00141)
*Ali Kargarandehkordi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究评估了在固定测量预算下，针对不同传感模态（心率、活动、生态瞬时评估）的自适应时间窗选择策略在纵向可穿戴数据集中的表现。结果显示，自适应策略在基线性能较低的参与者中显著提升预测性能（AUROC最高提升0.7），而在基线表现良好的参与者中收益有限甚至为负。自适应增益与基线性能呈强负相关（皮尔逊r = -0.67；斯皮尔曼p = -0.62）。大多数个体在AUROC上受益（60-80%），但F1得分改善较小且不一致。结论表明，自适应传感并非普遍有益，其最大价值体现在基线性能较差的场景中，支持根据基线表现定制部署策略以提高可穿戴健康监测效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解自适应传感策略在个体间的效果差异，优化在有限数据预算下的可穿戴健康系统预测性能，实现更高效的资源分配。

Method: 在纵向可穿戴数据集上，比较自适应选择时间窗与随机采样在心率、活动和生态瞬时评估（EMA）等多模态数据上的模型训练效果，使用AUROC和F1分数评估性能提升。

Result: 自适应策略在基线性能低的参与者中带来显著的AUROC提升（最高达0.7），而对基线表现好的参与者收益有限或为负；自适应增益与基线性能呈强负相关（皮尔逊r = -0.67；斯皮尔曼p = -0.62）；多数参与者（60-80%）在AUROC上获益，但F1提升较小且不一致。

Conclusion: 自适应传感并非对所有个体均有益，其最大价值在于基线性能较差的场景。应根据个体基线表现实施针对性的自适应传感部署，以提升可穿戴健康监测的效率。

Abstract: Adaptive sensing strategies that selectively sample data are increasingly used in wearable health systems to improve prediction performance under limited data budgets, yet their benefits across individuals remain poorly understood. Here, we evaluate adaptive selection of time windows for model training under fixed measurement budgets across multiple sensing modalities, including heart rate, activity, and ecological momentary assessment (EMA), in a longitudinal wearable dataset. We quantify performance gains relative to random sampling using both area under the receiver operating characteristic curve (AUROC) and F1 score. Adaptive strategies yield substantial improvements in AUROC for participants with low baseline performance (with gains up to 0.7), while offering limited or negative gains for participants with strong baselines. Across modalities, adaptive gain is strongly inversely correlated with baseline performance (Pearson r = -0.67; Spearman p = -0.62). At the participant level, most individuals benefit in AUROC (60-80% across modalities), although improvements in F1 are smaller and less consistent. These findings show that adaptive sensing is not uniformly beneficial, but instead provides the greatest value in underperforming settings. Our results support selective deployment strategies that tailor adaptive sensing based on baseline performance to improve efficiency in wearable health monitoring.

</details>


### [103] [BudgetDraft: Acceptance-Aware Multi-View Training for Sparse-KV Speculative Decoding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00144)
*Liang He,Jingbo Wen,Qishi Zhan,Yixiong Chen,Kangning Cui,Qizhen Lan,Xilu Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: BudgetDraft提出一种多视角稀疏训练方法，用于中长上下文（4K-16K）下的稀疏推测解码。通过在训练中让起草者接触多种采样的KV缓存预算，使其学习将每个稀疏视图与一个共享的全缓存教师目标对齐，从而提升不同稀疏度下的接受率。结合接受率感知损失与多视角损失，生成一个无需额外推理组件的、对预算鲁棒的起草者，在保持内存友好性的同时显著提升端到端速度，实验表明在4K、8K、16K上下文长度下分别实现最高6.55x、4.46x、2.10x加速。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在资源受限的部署环境中，稀疏KV缓存虽能控制峰值GPU内存和延迟，但随着上下文长度增长，稀疏/全量缓存之间的不匹配导致接受率迅速下降，限制了推测解码的效率。如何在中长上下文场景下维持高接受率并保持内存效率成为关键挑战。

Method: 提出BudgetDraft，采用多视角稀疏训练：在训练过程中，起草者被暴露于多个采样的KV缓存预算，学习将每个稀疏视图与统一的全缓存教师目标对齐。模型设计包含两个分支：全缓存分支引入接受率感知损失，稀疏缓存分支引入多视角损失，联合优化以生成对不同预算鲁棒的起草者。

Result: 在PG-19、LongBench和LWM数据集上，BudgetDraft在4K、8K、16K上下文长度下分别实现最高6.55x、4.46x、2.10x的端到端速度提升，同时保持推理管道的内存友好性，显著优于传统稀疏/全量推测解码方法。

Conclusion: BudgetDraft通过多视角稀疏训练有效缓解了中长上下文下稀疏/全量缓存不匹配问题，实现了高接受率与低内存开销的平衡，是资源受限场景下高效推测解码的重要进展。

Abstract: Speculative decoding speeds up autoregressive decoding by using a drafter to propose multiple tokens that a verifier validates in parallel. In resource-constrained deployments, the drafter uses a sparse KV cache to limit peak GPU memory and end-to-end latency under a fixed KV budget, while the verifier keeps a full KV cache. Mid-to-long context inference (4K--16K context length) is common in real applications. However, naive sparse/full speculative decoding suffers from the sparse/full mismatch as context length grows, causing the acceptance rate to drop quickly. We propose BudgetDraft, a multi-view sparse training method for sparse drafting in mid-to-long inference. The drafter is exposed to multiple sampled KV budgets during training and learns to align each sparse view with one shared full-cache teacher target. BudgetDraft combines an acceptance-aware loss on a full-cache branch with a multi-view loss on a sparse-cache branch, producing a single budget-robust drafter that recovers acceptance across sparsity levels without extra inference-time components. Experimental results on PG-19, LongBench, and LWM show that BudgetDraft achieves up to 6.55x, 4.46x, and 2.10x end-to-end speedup vs AR at 4K, 8K, and 16K context lengths, while keeping the inference pipeline memory-friendly.

</details>


### [104] [RAFT: Data Refinement and Adaptive Distillation for Domain Fine-Tuning with Alleviated Forgetting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00147)
*Yuduo Li,Xiaofeng Shi,Qian Kou,Longbin Yu,Hua Zhou*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: RAFT提出一种两阶段框架，通过数据重构与自适应蒸馏缓解领域微调中的遗忘问题。首先，通过自条件重写、语义过滤和答案融合构建与模型兼容的监督信号；其次，采用基于答案的在线策略蒸馏，使原模型在学生生成轨迹上提供软目标，并以融合答案为上下文进行指导。引入top-K温度蒸馏与EMA自适应损失平衡，稳定领域-通用性权衡。在三个指令调优基线和五个领域上，RAFT相比标准SFT平均提升领域准确率23.2%，并在MS-Bench和IFEval上分别恢复18.2%和10.2%的性能退化，证明了该方法在保留通用能力的同时有效提升领域性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 领域监督微调虽能提升特定领域的表现，但常导致模型通用能力下降。现有方法存在两个关键问题：监督不兼容（领域目标风格与原始响应不一致）和轨迹保真度缺失（教师强制训练未约束模型自身生成路径），从而破坏原有行为模式。因此需要一种既能增强领域适应性又可保护通用能力的新范式。

Method: RAFT采用两阶段设计：第一阶段通过自条件重写、语义过滤与答案融合生成与模型风格一致的高质量标注数据；第二阶段实施答案条件下的在线策略蒸馏（Answer-Conditioned On-Policy Distillation），利用原始模型对学生的生成路径提供软标签，同时以融合后的答案作为上下文引导，结合top-K温度蒸馏与基于EMA的自适应损失平衡机制，实现对模型行为轨迹的动态保持与性能优化。

Result: 在三个指令调优基线和五个不同领域上评估，RAFT相较标准SFT平均提升领域准确率23.2%；在通用评测集MS-Bench和IFEval上分别恢复18.2%和10.2%的性能损失，表明其在提升领域性能的同时显著缓解了通用能力的退化。

Conclusion: RAFT通过数据重构与轨迹级行为保持的协同设计，为领域微调提供了一种有效且稳健的方法。该框架不仅显著提升领域性能，还能有效缓解因微调带来的通用能力退化，验证了在监督兼容性和行为轨迹保真方面联合优化的重要性。

Abstract: Domain-specific supervised fine-tuning (SFT) often improves in-domain performance at the cost of degrading a model's general capabilities. We view this degradation through two practical gaps in domain SFT: a supervision-compatibility gap, where domain targets differ in style and reasoning format from the original model's natural responses, and a trajectory-preservation gap, where teacher-forced SFT optimizes fixed target tokens without constraining the model's behavior on its own generated prefixes. This process fails to preserve the model's original behavior. We propose RAFT (Data Refinement and Adaptive Distillation for Domain Fine-Tuning with Alleviated Forgetting), a two-stage framework that addresses both factors. First, RAFT constructs model-compatible supervision through self-conditioned rewriting, semantic filtering, and answer fusion. Second, RAFT performs Answer-Conditioned On-Policy Distillation, where the original instruction-tuned model provides soft targets on student-generated trajectories while being conditioned on the fused answer as helpful context. We further introduce top-K temperature distillation and EMA-based adaptive loss balancing to stabilize the domain-general trade-off. Across three instruction-tuned backbones and five domains, RAFT improves average domain accuracy by 23.2% over standard SFT, while recovering part of the SFT-induced degradation on MS-Bench and IFEval, with relative improvements of 18.2% and 10.2%, respectively. These results show that coupling data refinement with trajectory-level preservation provides an effective recipe for domain fine-tuning with alleviated forgetting.

### [105] [Emergence of Exploration in Policy Gradient Reinforcement Learning via Retrying](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00151)
*Soichiro Nishimori,Paavo Parmas,Sotetsu Koyamada,Tadashi Kozuno,Toshinori Kitamura,Shin Ishii,Yutaka Matsuo*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: ReMax提出一种新的目标函数，通过评估策略在M次采样中的期望最大回报来促进探索，无需显式奖励项。该方法导出了新的策略梯度公式，并引入了ReMax PPO（RePPO），可连续调节探索强度，实验证明其在MinAtar和Craftax基准上有效提升探索能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在强化学习中，探索的收益依赖于相似状态的重复出现；若无重复，贪婪策略最优。现有方法常依赖显式的探索奖励项，但可能引入偏差或不稳定性。本文旨在通过更自然的方式实现探索，避免人为设计的奖励机制。

Method: 提出ReMax目标函数，基于M次采样下的期望最大回报，并考虑回报不确定性；推导出相应的策略梯度更新规则；设计ReMax PPO（RePPO），将离散的重试次数M推广为连续参数m>0，实现对探索强度的精细控制。

Result: RePPO在MinAtar和Craftax基准上表现出良好的探索能力，且无需任何显式的探索奖励项，证明了其在复杂任务中有效引导探索的潜力。

Conclusion: ReMax通过期望最大回报建模，使探索成为策略优化的自然结果。RePPO作为其高效实现，提供了对探索强度的连续调控能力，在不依赖额外奖励的情况下显著提升了探索性能。

Abstract: In reinforcement learning (RL), agents benefit from exploration only because they repeatedly encounter similar states: trying different actions can improve performance or reduce uncertainty; without such retries, a greedy policy is optimal. We formalize this intuition with ReMax, an objective that evaluates a policy by the expected maximum return over $M$ samples, where $M$ is a positive integer, while accounting for return uncertainty. Optimizing this objective induces stochastic exploration as an emergent property, without explicit bonus terms. For efficient policy optimization, we derive a new policy-gradient formulation for ReMax and introduce ReMax PPO (RePPO), a PPO variant that optimizes ReMax while generalizing the discrete retry count $M$ to a continuous parameter $m > 0$, enabling fine-grained control of exploration. Empirically, RePPO promotes exploration, without any explicit exploration bonuses, on the MinAtar and Craftax benchmarks.

Despite the strong capacity of the latter to model complex temporal dynamics and inter-variable relationships, our results indicate that for churn prediction, conventional methods can still outperform it in terms of predictive performance, data efficiency, and computational resource requirements for training and deployment. These findings are consistent across multiple datasets and various churn labeling techniques.

### [107] [Beyond Augmentation: Score-Guided Pathological Prior for EEG-based Depression Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00180)
*Xiaojing Chen,Jingqi Cheng,Xu Zhao,Wan Jiang,Jingjing Wu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为"Beyond Augmentation: Score-Guided Classification (SGC)"的新框架，旨在解决基于深度学习的抑郁症（MDD）检测中因样本量小导致的挑战。该方法不依赖数据增强，而是通过无监督生成网络计算样本的结构与统计异常度作为病理先验，并将其融合到深度特征中以指导分类器决策边界。同时引入跨通道空间自适应模块，以应对多中心数据中设备异构问题。在Mumtaz2016和高密度MODMA数据集上的实验表明，该方法在零数据增强和零合成成本条件下仍具备优异性能和泛化能力。

Abstract: Deep learning-based Major Depressive Disorder (MDD) detection using Electroencephalography (EEG) is fundamentally constrained by the "small-sample dilemma." Prevailing generative data augmentation methods not only incur heavy computational overhead but also risk introducing synthetic noise, thereby blurring classification boundaries. To challenge the traditional "data quantity first" convention, we propose a novel framework "Beyond Augmentation": Score-Guided Classification (SGC). SGC does not synthesize pseudo-samples; instead, it utilizes an unsupervised generative network architecture to model the structural and statistical anomaly degrees of samples, serving as the core "Pathological Prior". This prior, after robust normalization, is explicitly fused with deep feature representations, thereby precisely guiding the classifier's decision boundary. Extensive experiments on the Mumtaz2016 and high-density MODMA datasets demonstrate the effectiveness and exceptional generalizability of our method under the challenging "zero data augmentation" setting and at "zero sample synthesis cost".

### [108] [Agentic Transformers Provably Learn to Search via Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00183)
*Tong Yang,Yu Huang,Yingbin Liang,Yuejie Chi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了基于Transformer的策略如何通过强化学习（RL）训练动态获得树搜索能力。在随机k叉树环境中，一个代理仅通过交互历史观察环境，并在到达隐藏的叶节点目标时获得终端奖励。研究构建了一个双头Transformer，实现随机深度优先搜索（DFS）：一个头追踪先前动作，另一个头检测失败并触发回溯。通过深度课程的策略梯度训练分析，发现这种DFS机制会分阶段从稀疏的强化反馈中自发出现，无需专家示范。训练后的策略表现出深度泛化能力——仅在深度1和2的树上训练后，即可成功应对更深的完整树。此外，在目标分布不平衡的情况下，折扣回报可导致优先选择高概率分支的排序DFS策略。总体而言，研究揭示了基于Transformer的搜索的一种机制性标准形式：注意力头通过专业化与协作，从上下文中提取决策相关轨迹，并通过RL训练将其转化为代理行为选择。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 模型在仅训练于深度1和2的树后，能成功处理更深的完整树，表现出深度泛化；在目标分布不均时，通过折扣回报生成优先访问高概率分支的排序DFS策略。

Abstract: Tree search is a central abstraction behind many language-agent reasoning and decision-making tasks: agents must explore actions, remember failures, and backtrack toward promising alternatives. Yet, we lack a theoretical understanding of how transformer-based policies acquire such search capabilities from the training dynamics of reinforcement learning (RL). We study this question in a stochastic $k$-ary tree environment, where an agentic transformer observes only its trajectory history through interaction and receives a terminal reward for reaching a hidden leaf goal node. We first construct a two-head transformer that implements randomized depth-first search (DFS): one head tracks previous actions, while the other detects failure outcomes and triggers backtracking. We then analyze the training dynamics of policy gradient under a depth-wise curriculum, showing that this same DFS mechanism emerges in stages from sparse reinforcement feedback without expert demonstrations. The resulting policy exhibits depth generalization: after training only on depth-$1$ and depth-$2$ trees, it succeeds on deeper full trees. We further show that, under imbalanced goal distributions, discounting the return leads to a ranked DFS policy that prioritizes higher-probability branches. Overall, our results identify a mechanistic normal form for transformer-based search, in which attention heads specialize and cooperate to extract decision-relevant traces from context and convert them into agentic action selection via RL training.

### [110] [Learning to Construct Practical Agentic Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00189)

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种设计和优化实用型代理系统的原则性方法，通过定义‘伪工具’实现模块化，使代理在受限上下文中递归调用LLM。研究发现，与动态规划的工作流相比，手工构建的固定工作流通常成本更低且更准确。进一步提出了针对伪工具和固定工作流的新学习方法，其性能优于手工设计的代理。利用框架的模块性，还应用多目标优化方法联合优化成本与响应质量，并融合多个学习系统的成果。

Method: 提出基于‘伪工具’的代理框架，支持模块化设计；采用手工构建固定工作流；开发新型学习方法训练伪工具与工作流；利用框架的模块性进行多目标优化并融合多个学习系统的结果。

Conclusion: 该框架为设计高效、可控、低成本的实用型代理系统提供了有效路径，结合学习与优化方法显著提升了系统性能与实用性。

Abstract: Automated design and optimization of agentic LLM-based systems leads to sophisticated systems that substantially improve result quality over off-the-shelf agentic patterns. However, studies of fielded agentic systems show that production systems focus much more on issues such as simplicity, controllability, and predictability of inference costs. In this paper we propose principled approaches to designing and optimizing practical agentic systems. We describe an agent framework that enables designers to enforce modularity in agentic systems, by defining "pseudo-tools" that call LLMs recursively on a restricted context. Using this framework we hand-engineer agents for a diverse set of tasks, and show that relative to dynamically-planned workflows, hand-constructed fixed workflows are generally cheaper and more accurate. We then propose novel learning methods for the agentic components required by this framework, namely pseudo-tools and fixed workflows. These learning methods generally outperform hand-engineered agents. We also exploit the modularity of the framework to apply multi-objective optimization methods to jointly optimize cost and response quality and blend the results of multiple learning systems.

### [111] [BAGEN: Are LLM Agents Budget-Aware?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00198)
*Yuxiang Lin,Zihan Wang,Mengyang Liu,Yuxuan Shan,Longju Bai,Junyao Zhang,Xing Jin,Boshan Chen,Jinyan Su,Xingyao Wang,Jiaxin Pei,Manling Li*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种预算感知智能体（BAGEN），将预算视为主动控制信号而非被动成本度量。通过区分内部预算（来自代理计算）和外部预算（来自代理行为），作者形式化了预算感知为渐进式区间估计：在计划的每一步预测剩余预算的上下界，并在完成可能性低时发出警告。实验发现，强模型不一定具备强预算感知能力（相关性r=0.35），前沿模型普遍过度乐观，持续投入失败任务而不及时预警。引入滚动重放评分协议后，早期停止可节省28-64%的令牌，且通过监督微调+强化学习（SFT+RL）可增强早期停止与预警行为。但区间校准仍具挑战，覆盖率最高仅达47%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前智能体资源消耗增加，但预算通常仅在执行后才被衡量，缺乏对预算的主动管理。为提升智能体效率与可靠性，需将预算作为动态控制信号，实现更智能的资源调度与风险预警。

Method: 定义内部与外部预算；提出渐进式区间估计方法，用于实时预测剩余预算范围并触发预警；采用滚动重放协议评估不同智能体的预算感知性能；使用SFT+RL训练模型以优化早期停止和预警行为。

Result: 实验显示：1）强模型不等于高预算感知（相关性仅0.35）；2）前沿模型普遍存在过度乐观倾向，延迟预警；3）预算感知信号可被有效训练，早期停止显著减少资源浪费（节省28-64%令牌）；4）区间校准难度大，覆盖率最高仅47%。

Conclusion: 预算应被视为智能体决策中的主动控制信号。尽管预算感知能力可通过训练提升，但精确的区间校准仍是关键挑战。未来工作需聚焦于提高预算预测的准确性与鲁棒性。

Abstract: While agents are increasingly spending more resources, today agent cost is mostly measured only after execution. A Budget-Aware Agent (BAGEN) should treat budget as an active control signal, rather than a passive cost metric. We first systematically define budget estimation as internal budgets (from agent computation) and external budgets (from agent actions). We then formalize budget-awareness as progressive interval estimation: at each step of a plan, an agent should predict an upper and lower bound on remaining budget, and alert when completion is unlikely. Scoring with a rollout-replay protocol, we find consistent failure patterns on four environments and five frontier agents: (1) strong agents do not necessarily have strong budget-awareness, with correlation r=0.35. (2) frontier models are consistently over-optimistic, continue spending on tasks that are unlikely to succeed, instead of alerting the user early. (3) budget-aware signal is actionable and trainable. Early stop saves 28-64% tokens on failed trajectories, and SFT+RL strengthens early stop and alert behavior. (4) precise interval calibration remains challenging, with interval coverage capping at 47% after SFT+RL. Project page: https://ragen-ai.github.io/bagen/

</details>


### [112] [From Rashomon Theory to PRAXIS: Efficient Decision Tree Rashomon Sets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00202)
*Zakk Heile,Hayden McTavish,Varun Babbar,Margo Seltzer,Cynthia Rudin*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: PRAXIS 是一种用于近似计算 Rashomon 集合的算法，显著提升了运行时间和内存使用效率，可有效应用于真实世界数据集，且能几乎完全恢复完整的 Rashomon 集合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准机器学习流程中存在大量近优模型，形成 Rashomon 集合，虽带来不确定性感知和鲁棒决策的机会，但其计算成本极高，尤其在简单可解释模型（如稀疏决策树）中仍需巨大资源。因此需要高效算法来近似该集合。

Method: 提出 PRAXIS 算法，通过优化策略近似计算 Rashomon 集合，大幅降低内存与运行时间开销。

Result: PRAXIS 在保持高精度的同时，实现数个数量级的性能提升，能够有效恢复几乎全部的完整 Rashomon 集合。

Conclusion: PRAXIS 为研究人员和实践者提供了可扩展的方法，用于在真实数据上建模 Rashomon 集合，推动了不确定性建模与可解释性决策的发展。

Abstract: Standard machine learning pipelines often admit many near-optimal models. These "Rashomon sets" pose a range of challenges and opportunities for uncertainty-aware, robust decision making. They allow users to incorporate domain knowledge and preferences that would otherwise be difficult to specify directly in an objective, and they quantify diversity among valid models for a given training dataset and objective function. However, computation of Rashomon sets, even for simple, interpretable model classes such as sparse decision trees, continues to require immense memory and runtime resources. We present PRAXIS, an algorithm to approximate this Rashomon set with orders of magnitude improvement in runtime and memory usage. We validate that PRAXIS regularly recovers almost all of the full Rashomon set. PRAXIS allows researchers and practitioners to scalably model the Rashomon set for real-world datasets. Code for PRAXIS is available at https://github.com/zakk-h/PRAXIS

### [113] [Quantized Reasoning Models Think They Need to Think Longer, but They Do Not](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00206)
*Sanae Lotfi,Polina Kirichenko,Steven Li,Zechun Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了后训练量化（PTQ）对大语言模型推理性能的影响，发现激进的量化会降低准确率并增加思维链（CoT）长度。令人惊讶的是，高达52%的量化模型失败案例中，模型在中间推理步骤中已得出正确答案，但未将其作为最终答案输出。通过分析量化前后输出分布的token级KL散度，发现高KL值位置与高下一个词熵相关，并且这些位置上量化模型更倾向于采样如"wait"、"but"、"alternatively"等过度思考标记。提出一种无需训练的logit惩罚方法，针对特定过度思考标记进行优化，可减少12-23%的CoT长度，同时保持或提升准确率，在5个模型（1.5B-32B参数）、3种量化方法和5个基准测试中表现优异，显著降低了量化导致的过度思考错误（最高减少58%）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解后训练量化（PTQ）对大语言模型推理能力的影响，特别是其如何引发过度思考错误，进而影响模型准确性与推理效率。

Method: 通过测量量化前后输出分布的token级KL散度，识别出易产生过度思考的高风险位置；设计一种无需训练的logit惩罚策略，对特定过度思考标记施加抑制，以减少不必要的推理步骤。

Result: 该方法在5个不同规模的模型（1.5B-32B参数）、3种量化方式和5个基准任务上均实现12-23%的CoT长度缩减，同时保持或提升准确率，显著减少了量化引起的过度思考错误（最多下降58%），构建了更优的准确率与推理成本权衡关系。

Conclusion: 量化虽带来部署效率优势，但会诱发过度思考错误，尤其在中间推理阶段出现正确答案却未输出的问题。通过引入仅需少量调整的训练自由logit惩罚机制，能有效缓解此问题，提升量化模型的推理质量与效率，为高效部署大模型提供新路径。

Abstract: Post-training quantization (PTQ) is widely used to deploy large language models efficiently, but its effect on reasoning models is not well understood. Across math, coding, and science QA, we find that aggressive PTQ reduces accuracy while increasing chain-of-thought (CoT) length. Surprisingly, we show that in up to 52% of the quantized models' failures, models reach the right answer in intermediate reasoning steps but do not output it as a final answer. To understand why quantization leads to this increase in overthinking errors, we measure the token-level KL divergence between quantized and full-precision output distributions. Positions with high KL divergence correlate strongly with high next-token entropy, and at these positions quantized models disproportionately sample overthinking markers such as "wait", "but", and "alternatively". We show that simply introducing a training-free logit penalty on a curated set of overthinking markers can reduce CoT length by 12--23% while preserving or improving accuracy across 5 models (1.5B-32B parameters), 3 quantization methods, and 5 benchmarks, yielding a favorable Pareto frontier of accuracy against reasoning cost compared to penalizing other token sets. Overthinking errors produced by quantized models are particularly reduced by up to 58%.

</details>


### [114] [LithoGRPO: Fast Inverse Lithography via GRPO Reinforced Flow Matching](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00228)
*Yao Lai,Xuyuan Xiong,Zeyue Xue,Guojin Chen,Jing Wang,Xihui Liu,Rui Zhang,Robert Mullins,Bei Yu,Ping Luo*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: LithoGRPO 是一种结合流匹配与基于 GRPO 的强化学习微调的逆光刻技术框架，用于在复杂工艺约束下高效生成高保真度掩模。通过引入快速计数算法，实现超过130倍的制造可行性评估加速，同时保持掩模排序准确性。实验表明，该方法在性能上超越现有优化和学习方法，兼具高效性与先进性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统逆光刻技术依赖物理指标评估掩模，限制了生成模型的应用；现有方法难以在复杂工艺约束下高效探索多样掩模设计。因此需要一种既能利用物理先验又能高效生成高质量掩模的新框架。

Method: LithoGRPO 采用流匹配生成初始掩模，并结合基于 GRPO 的强化学习进行微调，利用物理定义的奖励函数优化掩模以满足工艺约束。同时提出快速计数算法，显著提升制造可行性评估效率。

Result: LithoGRPO 在多个基准测试中达到当前最优性能，相比优化与学习方法均表现更优，且掩模生成速度显著提升，具备工业应用潜力。

Conclusion: LithoGRPO 是首个将流匹配与强化学习统一于掩模优化的框架，通过高效采样与物理感知优化，实现了高质量、高效率的逆光刻设计，为半导体制造中的高精度图案转移提供了新范式。

Abstract: In semiconductor manufacturing, lithography projects circuit layouts onto silicon wafers through an optical mask. As circuit features shrink below the wavelength of light, optical diffraction causes the printed patterns to deviate from their intended layouts. Inverse Lithography Technology (ILT) addresses this challenge by generating optimized masks that enhance the fidelity of pattern transfer onto wafers. While ILT resembles an image synthesis task, its reliance on explicit physical metrics for mask evaluation limits the applicability of existing generative models. We introduce LithoGRPO, an ILT framework that integrates the flow-matching paradigm with GRPO-based reinforcement learning (RL) fine-tuning, enabling efficient exploration of diverse masks for a given target layout. Unlike purely generative or optimization-based approaches, RL in LithoGRPO exploits the explicitly defined, physics-based reward function of ILT, enabling optimization under complex, process-aware constraints. To the best of our knowledge, this is the first framework that unifies flow matching and RL for mask optimization. To improve RL sampling efficiency, we propose a fast shot-counting algorithm for manufacturability evaluation, achieving over 130x speedup while preserving the mask ranking of the traditional shot-count metric. Extensive experiments demonstrate that LithoGRPO achieves state-of-the-art performance over both optimization-based and learning-based methods, while maintaining efficient mask generation.

### [115] [A Pre-Training Analogue of Grokking in Language Models: Tracing Delayed Grammatical Generalization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00230)
*Sherin Muckatira,Namrata Shivagunde,Vijeta Deshpande,Anna Rumshisky*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于暴露度的框架，用于研究大语言模型预训练过程中的类grokking现象。通过BLiMP最小对数据集，识别关键短语并划分代理训练/验证集，发现延迟泛化现象；模型在泛化后，语法概念向量更可预测语法正确性，占据更高维子空间，且注意力集中在少数注意力头上。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究多关注监督学习中神经网络在大量迭代后的泛化现象（grokking），但大语言模型预训练采用无标签语料的下个词预测任务，数据重复少、无明确训练/验证划分，难以直接研究此类动态。因此需要新的框架来探索预训练中的延迟泛化行为。

Method: 提出暴露度框架：基于BLiMP最小对数据集，识别每个句子的关键短语（最小连续跨度，体现语法差异和上下文信息），将关键短语出现在预训练窗口内的样本划为代理训练集，其余为代理验证集，从而构建可评估的泛化分析环境。

Result: 在五种语法现象中均观察到延迟泛化；预训练检查点分析显示，泛化后语法概念向量对语法可接受性的预测能力增强，所占子空间维度更高；注意力机制显示关键词到相关上下文词的注意力集中于少数注意力头。

Conclusion: 大语言模型预训练中存在类似grokking的延迟泛化现象，其背后是语法表示的逐渐优化与注意力机制的聚焦，表明模型在长期训练中逐步掌握深层语法结构。

Abstract: Grokking, the phenomenon in which neural networks generalize long after fitting their training data, has been studied in supervised settings on many epochs. LLM pre-training instead involves next-token prediction over an unlabeled corpus, with limited data repetition and no explicit train/validation split. To address this, we propose an exposure-based framework that enables the study of grokking-like dynamics during LLM pre-training. We ground our evaluation in BLiMP minimal pairs, which provide controlled grammatical contrasts. For every BLiMP minimal pair, we identify a critical phrase, the smallest continuous span that captures the grammatical contrast and the phenomenon-relevant context. Examples whose critical phrase appears in the pre-training window are assigned to the proxy-train split; the remaining examples are assigned to the proxy-validation split. Across five grammatical phenomena, we observe delayed generalization. Analyzing pre-training checkpoints before and after generalization shows that grammatical concept vectors become more predictive of grammatical acceptability and occupy a higher-dimensional subspace after generalization. We also find that attention from the critical token to the relevant context token is concentrated in a small number of heads.

### [116] [InfoAtlas: A Foundation Model for Zero-Shot Statistical Dependence Estimate](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00241)
*Zhengyang Hu,Yanzhi Chen,Hanxiang Ren,Qunsong Zeng,Youyi Zheng,Adrian Weller,Kaibin Huang,Yanchao Yang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: InfoAtlas 是一种类似基础模型的架构，通过在大规模合成数据上预训练，能够在单次前向传播中直接推断互信息（MI），显著提升速度（100倍加速），同时保持与现有先进神经估计器相当的准确性。它能灵活处理不同维度和样本量，并在复杂真实场景中表现出良好泛化能力，将MI估计转化为推理任务，为实时依赖分析奠定基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统神经互信息（MI）估计器需要针对每个新数据集进行代价高昂的迭代优化，难以应用于实时场景。因此亟需一种高效、通用且可快速推理的MI估计方法。

Method: InfoAtlas 采用预训练的神经网络架构，在大规模合成数据上学习多样化的依赖结构，通过单次前向传播直接预测给定数据集的互信息，无需迭代优化。

Result: 实验表明，InfoAtlas 在准确率上媲美最先进的神经估计器，速度提升达100倍；能够统一处理不同维度和样本量的数据，并在真实复杂场景中实现良好泛化。

Conclusion: 通过将互信息估计转化为推理任务，InfoAtlas 有效解决了传统方法的计算瓶颈，为实时高维依赖分析提供了可行方案，具有广泛的应用前景。

Abstract: Measuring statistical dependency between high-dimensional random variables is a fundamental task in data science and machine learning. Neural mutual information (MI) estimators offer a promising avenue, but they typically require costly iterative optimization for each new dataset, making them impractical for real-time applications. We present InfoAtlas, a foundation model-like architecture that eliminates this bottleneck by directly inferring MI in a single forward pass. Pretrained on large-scale synthetic data with rich dependence patterns, InfoAtlas learns to identify diverse dependence structures and predict MI directly from the dataset. Comprehensive experiments demonstrate that InfoAtlas matches state-of-the-art neural estimators in accuracy while achieving $100\times$ speedup, can flexibly handle varying dimensions and sample sizes through a single unified model, and generalizes effectively to complex, real-world scenarios. By reformulating MI estimation as an inference task, InfoAtlas establishes a foundation for real-time dependency analysis.
